there be a soothing authoritative UNSCEAR ( United Nation Scientific Committee on the Effect of Atomic Radiation ) report in 2000 on the health effect of Chernobyl confirm that there be no scientific evidence of any significant radiation - related health effect to most people expose .
this be heavily promote by the Australasian Radiation Protection Society in a press release title the MYTHS of CHERNOBYL which contain the follow :
one of the most widespread myth of recent time be that the Chernobyl nuclear reactor accident in 1986 cause many thousand of extra cancer death in neighbour region , and that public health have be severely affect by exposure to radiation .
many people still believe that to be true , even though the Ministry of Russian federation on Civil Defence , Emergency and Elimination of Conseguence of Natural Disaster ( EMERCOM of Russia ) report this in 1996 :
CHERNOBYL accident : ten year on
in the last decade , there have be a real and significant increase in childhood and , to a certain extent , adult carcinoma of the thyroid in contaminate region of the former Soviet Union ( Wi940 ) which should be attribute to the Chernobyl accident until prove otherwise .
the prestigious IAEA ( International Atomic Energy Agency ) publish a early report on Chernobyl which be base on information from Russian source and state that there be no significant health effect .
however , in April 2001 , the IAEA publish Fifteen Year after the Chernobyl Accident - Lesson learn . which contradict the early report .
here be some excerpt :
the dramatic increase in radiation - induce thyroid cancer in child and adolescent in Belarus , Russia , and Ukraine , which have be observe since 1991 , continue to this day .
... a drop in the birth rate , a deterioration in _ reproductive health , a increase in complication during pregnancy and birth , and a deterioration in neonatal health ....
the dynamics of change in the state of health of child affect by the Chernobyl accident in all three country - Belarus , Russia , and Ukraine - in the post-accident period be characterize by persistent negative tendency : the morbidity rate be go up , the number of really healthy child be drop , and disability be increase .

from _ Daily Star
by Juan Cole
Friday , June 04 , 2004
as the American public gradually weary of the Iraq crisis , some have begin worry that the war could blow back on the US by create the condition for anti-American terrorism .
Israel , however , be much close to Iraq and be likely to suffer from Iraqi instability much more acutely than will the United State .
ironically , among the strong proponent of war in Iraq be Israeli Prime Minister Ariel Sharon and he neoconservative supporter in the US .
have they , however , actually weaken Israeli security ?
the big threat Israel face be not from conventional army but from the asymmetrical tactic of Palestinian national liberation movement .
the derailing of the Oslo peace process by the hard - line policy of Sharon and the Palestinian intifada have encourage suicide bombing .
this , in turn , have discourage international investment in Israel and have make it less likely that immigrant to the country will actually remain there .
although Israel withdraw from Lebanese territory in May 2000 , the radical Lebanese Shiite party , Hizbullah , have not be mollify .
it be estimate to have some 5000 armed fighter , and they have pursue attack against Israeli force to compel they to withdraw from the Shebaa Farm , a sliver of Syrian territory that Israel annex after the 1967 war .
any thorough assessment of the impact of the Iraq war and its aftermath on _ security environment must , therefore , closely examine its likely effect on the conduct of asymmetrical warfare .
although it be often allege ( without much evidence ) that Saddam Hussein give money to the family of Palestinian suicide bomber and so encourage asymmetrical warfare , it be not clear that he actually pose a danger to Israel .
the Palestinian who have be willing to kill themselves to end the Israeli occupation of the Gaza Strip and the West Bank be not drive by economic consideration .
Saddam never do anything practical to help the Palestinian .
at some point , as in the late 1980 , he reportedly make behind - the - scene overture to the Israeli to arrive at some sort of a deal .
he do not allow Palestinian radical to launch operation against Israel from Iraq .
by the late 1990 , Iraq have no nuclear or biological weapon program , and have destroy its chemical weapon stockpile .
its ramshackle army have virtually collapse before the American invasion in 2003 .
if it be hard to see how Baathist Iraq pose any real threat to Israel , it be not so difficult to see a menace in the current instability .
the bungling of post-war Iraq by the Bush administration create a weak and fail state .
armed militia , many staff by former Iraqi military man with substantial training and experience , have proliferate .
the US choose to ally itself with such group as the Supreme Council for the Islamic Revolution in Iraq , whose 15000 - strong Badr Corps paramilitary be train by the Iranian Revolutionary Guard .
anti-Israeli and pro-Palestinian feeling be strong among several major Iraqi ideological group and current .
the more radical Shiite , who generally follow the theocratic notion of _ Ayatollah Ruhollah Khomeini , routinely chant and demonstrate against Israel .
they vehemently protest the Israeli assassination of Sheikh Ahmed Yassin , the leader of Hamas , last March .
bad for Israel , the assassination draw a denunciation even from the moderate and cautious Grand Ayatollah Ali Sistani , who wield enormous moral authority over Iraqi Shiite .
this Shiite movement have be suppress by Saddam _ regime , but have now organize and arm themselves .
they have also reestablish they historical link with Lebanese and Iranian Shiite .
it be inevitable that most Iraqi Shiite will side with they Hizbullah coreligionist against Israel , and it seem likely that Iraqi Shiite will get rich enough from Iraqi petroleum sale in the future that they will be in a good position to bankroll Lebanese Shiite radical .
Sunni Arab fundamentalist deeply sympathize with the Palestinian and with Hamas , and that in Iraq have deep historical ink with fundamentalist in Jordan and Palestine .
Iraqi city such as Fallujah and Ramadi be on the truck route from Amman to Baghdad , and so come under the influence of the Salafi movement , which be popular in Jordan .
secular Arab nationalist group also universally sympathize with the Palestinian , and that in post-saddam Iraq be no exception .
whereas Saddam _ dictatorship ensure that such populist current be keep firmly under control , they be now free to organize .
a Iraq in which armed fundamentalist and nationalist militia proliferate be inevitably a security worry for Israel .
if even a modicum of normality and security can be return to Iraq , its citizen will be able to benefit from the _ petroleum reserve .
that private wealth can easily be funnel into aid for the Palestinian and for Lebanese Shiite .
_ security interest be well serve by peace with its neighbor , which can only be achieve by trade land for peace with the Palestinian .
Ariel _ aggressive near annexation of almost half of the occupy West Bank and he indefinite postponement of any Palestinian state have create unprecedented rage and violence .
the anger have spread throughout the Muslim world , include Iraq .
the promotion by the pro-Zionist right of twin occupation - in the West Bank and in Iraq - have profoundly weaken , not strengthen , Israeli security .
Juan Cole ( www.juancole.com ) be a professor of modern Middle East history at the University of Michigan and author of " Sacred Space and Holy War " ( I.B. Tauris , 2002 ) .
the DAILY STAR publish this commentary in agreement with Agence Global
Tamil feel that the propose defense agreement between India and Sri Lanka would encourage Sinhala ruler to prepare for another war abandon the current peace process
but there be strong hint in the country that a new Indo - Sri Lanka defense deal could be in the making .
and this have already draw protest from the Tamil National Alliance ( TNA ) which be back by the LTTE in the April general election hold in Sri Lanka .
apart from the 1200 Indian life lose in 1987 , the Indian peacekeeping force be immensely unpopular not only in Tamil Nadu and the Jaffna peninsula but also among the Sinhalese majority who consider it a violation of they _ sovereignty .
India defensive over Sri Lanka
by Ranjit Devraj
NEW DELHI -
while India be ready to enter into a " defense cooperation agreement " with Sri Lanka , it be wary of be draw into any military involvement in the island _ two decade - old civil war that have see violent strife between ethnic Tamil and the Sinhalese majority - leave over 60000 dead on both side .
and that explain the delay in the signing of a formal defense agreement that be at the heart of sri lankan President Chandrika _ four - day visit to India recently .
accord to Professor S D Muni , South Asia expert at the Jawaharal Nehru University , the two - year peace talk between Colombo and the Liberation Tiger of Tamil Eelam ( LTTE ) be stalemate .
for that reason , he say , _ government be keen to beef up military preparedness with Indian support .
" the sri lankan government do not want to initiate a conflict but would be interested in deter the LTTE from start one .
and the Tiger look as if they be on the brink of launch another offensive , " Muni tell IPS .
Colombo hold six round of talk with the Tiger between September 2002 and March 2003 .
but last April , the rebel abruptly pull out of negotiation demand recognition , first , for the right to self - rule before proceed any further .
_ India tour precede a three - day visit to Sri Lanka by Norwegian Foreign Minister Jan Petersen in a new bid to revive the peace talk that be suppose to follow a ceasefire that Oslo successfully broker in February 2002 .
Petersen hold discussion with both Kumaratunga and the reclusive LTTE leader Velupillai Prabhakaran in the rebel stronghold of Kilinochchi without success , and chief Tamil rebel negotiator Anton Balasingham and Norwegian envoy Erik Solheim hold close - door talk at the international airport late Saturday in a effort to keep the salvage effort on track , diplomatic source say .
but they , too , fail .
Colombo , too , seem to be in a intractable position .
accord to former Indian army general A S Kalkat , the difficulty for _ government lay in the fact that the LTTE have become a de jure power in the north and east of the island and be run every aspect of civil administration in the area within its control .
a veteran of _ military intervention in the Jaffna peninsula to help implement the 1987 Indo - Sri Lanka Peace Accord - which ambitiously provide for the disarming of the formidable LTTE - Kalkat say the new defense deal would essentially be a reiteration of the old one minus its military commitment .
Kalkat , who currently chair the independent US - base International Council on Conflict Resolution , say despite the failure of the Indian army to disarm or even subdue the Tiger , India remain the only power capable of influence the course of the current peace talk .
" the Norwegian mean well but they role be limited to that of honest broker and the LTTE be keenly aware that they do not have the power [ unlike India ] to underwrite any arrangement , " Kalkat tell IPS in a interview .
in 1987 , the Tamil Tiger reluctantly accept the peace accord under Indian pressure .
under the accord , a new northeastern provincial council be form and the Indian army be deploy as peacekeeper in the north and east .
however , difference between India and LTTE soon surface and lead to clash between Tiger guerrilla and the Indian peace keeping force .
about 1200 Indian soldier be kill during this phase of the conflict .
India have to pull back its force from Sri Lanka in 1989 follow the election of Ranasinghe Premadasa , a strong critic of Indian mediation .
last June , a international initiative lead by Japan to persuade the LTTE to come back to the negotiating table fail despite a aid package offer of US$ 4.5 billion .
_ special envoy , Yasushi Akashi , who call for tangible progress in the peace process before the money would be release , come back from visit to Colombo and Kilinochchi in early November a frustrated man .
he complain about the " visible lack of progress " and reach a impasse in talk with both side .
the _ chief ideologue , Balasingham , sniff at the proposal say that " a solution to the ethnic conflict _ be predetermine by the resolution or declaration of donor conference , but have to be negotiate by the party in conflict without the constraint of external force . "
but there be strong hint in the country that a new Indo - Sri Lanka defense deal could be in the making .

trouble on _ island
Ramtanu Maitra
in early February , India charge 34 arakan separatist from Myanmar with hide in the Landfall Island , part of the Andaman Island group ( see end note ) .
this alleged member of the Arakan Army , the military wing of the National Unity Party in Myanmar , have be charge with illegal entry .
it be likely , but not certain , that they will be deport to Myanmar .
but the news of the arakan rebel be just the tip of the iceberg when it come to grow concern in New Delhi over the security of the Andaman Island .
report be circulate in the intelligence community that the Andaman Island be not only thick with Myanmar rebel .
it have also become a arm depot of the Liberation Tiger of Tamil Eelam ( LTTE ) , who operate almost freely in the Andaman Sea .
information point in this direction come to light after the December 26 tsunami , which take a heavy toll on the Andaman .
correspondent who flock in to cover the tsunami find they also have another story - the miserable security situation surround the Indian _ Far Eastern Naval Command , now be establish along with _ " blue water navy " .
deteriorate security
security problem in the Andaman Sea be not new , but they have deteriorate during the past few year , in tandem with a deterioration in the security situation in Bangladesh , Nepal and Bhutan , and particularly in the northeastern Indian state of Manipur , Nagaland and Tripura .
while the Indian army have become rock - solid in the western front , and have develop the capability of withstand any Pakistani adventure in that sector , it have become highly vulnerable in its eastern sector , where its enemy be not a national army but a multitude of secessionist , terrorist and drug - run militant operate between Southeast Asia and northeastern India through Bangladesh .
the Andaman Sea be a major conduit for this traffic , and the 572 large and small island that constitute the Andaman and Nicobar group be a natural transit base .
the drug and arm travel in all direction .
since the " Sea Tiger " of the LTTE , well know as the Tamil Tiger , be the one who rule the Andaman Sea : they carry the arm and drug for they own use and also to deliver to rebel in Aceh and all along the east coast of Africa .
it be old news that the Tamil Tiger have develop a strong network within South Africa .
this be not unknown to New Delhi .
a recent report by a journalist from Port Blair , in the Andaman , quote a unnamed official say that foreigner from Myanmar , Bangladesh and Sri Lanka have permanently settle in the island , use fake Indian ration card , while citizen of Thailand , China , Indonesia and Malaysia have migrate temporarily to plunder the natural resource and leave .
" Port Blair , Havelock Island , Diglipur , Middle Nicobar , _ Bay , Neil Island and Rangott be mostly overrun by foreigner , " he say .
a official estimate issue in 2003 suggest there be 50000 " foreigner " in the Andaman Island , but unofficial figure be much high than this .
a large number of they be Bangladeshi , who like million of they countryman have leave they densely populate homeland to settle elsewhere .
as most of they have few technical skill , and the Andaman have little demand for they in any case , they turn to smuggling and other unlawful activity .
the presence of the Sea Tiger in the area with gun , cash and drug make the situation extremely dangerous .
report from Port Blair make it evident that New Delhi get little on - the - ground intelligence , and the Indian Coast Guard be grossly unequipped to deal with the surge of illegal migrant to the island .
one unnamed naval officer be quote say , " arm smuggling be a very profitable business in this region . "
consider the _ huge strategic importance , it be amazing how lax New Delhi have be .

note

" a View from the Eye of the Storm "
talk deliver by Haim Harari at a meeting of the International Advisory Board of a large multi-national corporation , April , 2004 :
" as you know , I usually provide the scientific and technological " entertainment " in we meeting , but , on this occasion , we Chairman suggest that I present my own personal view on event in the part of the world from which I come .
I have never be and I will never be a government official and I have no privileged information .
my perspective be entirely base on what I see , on what I read and on the fact that my family have live in this region for almost 200 year .
you may regard my view as that of the proverbial taxi driver , which you be suppose to question , when you visit a country .
I could have share with you some fascinating fact and some personal thought about the Israeli - Arab conflict .
however , I will touch upon it only in passing .
I prefer to devote most of my remark to the broad picture of the region and its place in world event .
I refer to the entire area between Pakistan and Morocco , which be predominantly Arab , predominantly Moslem , but include many non-Arab and also significant non-Moslem minority .
why do I put aside Israel and its own immediate neighborhood ?
because Israel and any problem related to it , in spite of what you might read or hear in the world media , be not the central issue , and have never be the central issue in the upheaval in the region .
yes , there be a 100 year - old Israeli - Arab conflict , but it be not where the main show be .
the million who die in the Iran - Iraq war have nothing to do with Israel .
the mass murder happen right now in Sudan , where the Arab Moslem regime be massacre its black Christian citizen , have nothing to do with Israel .
the frequent report from Algeria about the murder of hundred of civilian in one village or another by other Algerian have nothing to do with Israel .
Saddam Hussein do not invade Kuwait , endanger Saudi Arabia and butcher he own people because of Israel .
Egypt do not use poison gas against Yemen in the 60' because of Israel .
Assad the Father do not kill ten of thousand of he own citizen in one week in El Hamma in Syria because of Israel .
the Taliban control of Afghanistan and the civil war there have nothing to do with Israel .
the Libyan blowing up of the Pan - Am flight have nothing to do with Israel , and I could go on and on and on .
the root of the trouble be that this entire Moslem region be totally dysfunctional , by any standard of the word , and would have be so even if Israel have join the Arab league and a independent Palestine have exist for 100 year .
the 22 member country of the Arab league , from Mauritania to the Gulf State , have a total population of 300 million , large than the US and almost as large as the EU before its expansion .
they have a land area large than either the US or all of Europe .
this 22 country , with all they oil and natural resource , have a combine GDP small than that of Netherlands plus Belgium and equal to half of the GDP of California alone .
within this meager GDP , the gap between rich and poor be beyond belief and too many of the rich make they money not by succeed in business , but by be corrupt ruler .
the social status of woman be far below what it be in the Western World 150 year ago .
human rights be below any reasonable standard , in spite of the grotesque fact that Libya be elect chair of the UN Human Right commission .
accord to a report prepare by a committee of Arab intellectual and publish under the auspices of the U.N. , the number of book translate by the entire Arab world be much small than what little Greece alone translate .
the total number of scientific publication of 300 million Arab be less than that of 6 million Israeli .
birth rate in the region be very high , increase the poverty , the social gap and the cultural decline .
and all of this be happen in a region , which only 30 year ago , be believe to be the next wealthy part of the world , and in a Moslem area , which develop , at some point in history , one of the most advanced culture in the world .
it be fair to say that this create a unprecedented breeding ground for cruel dictator , terror network , fanaticism , incitement , suicide murder and general decline .
it be also a fact that almost everybody in the region blame this situation on the United State , on Israel , on western civilization , on Judaism and Christianity , on anyone and anything , except themselves .
a word about the million of decent , honest , good people who be either devout Moslem or be not very religious but grow up in Moslem family : they be double victim of a outside world , which now develop islamophobia , and of they own environment which break they heart by be totally dysfunctional .
the problem be that the vast silent majority of this Moslem be not part of the terror and the incitement , but they also do not stand up against it .
they become accomplice , by omission , and this apply to political leader , intellectual , business people and many other .
many of they can certainly tell right from wrong , but be afraid to express they view .
the event of the last few year have amplify four issue , which have always exist , but have never be as rampant as in the present upheaval in the region .
a few more year may pass before everybody acknowledge that it be a World War , but we be already well into it .
this be the four main pillar of the current world conflict , or perhaps we should already refer to it as " the undeclared World War III " :
* 1 . the first element be the suicide murder . *
suicide murder be not a new invention but they have be make popular , if I may use this expression , only lately .
even after September 11 , it seem that most of the Western World do not yet understand this weapon .
it be a very potent psychological weapon .
its real direct impact be relatively minor .
the total number of casualty from hundred of suicide murder within Israel in the last three year be much small than that due to car accident .
September 11 be quantitatively much less lethal than many earthquake
more people die from aids in one day in Africa than all the Russian who die in the hand of Chechnya - base Moslem suicide murderer since that conflict start .
Saddam kill every month more people than all that who die from suicide murder since the Coalition occupation of Iraq .
so what be all the fuss about suicide killing ?
it create headline .
it be spectacular .
it be frightening .
it be a very cruel death with body dismember and horrible severe lifelong injury to many of the wounded .
it be always show on television in great detail .
one such murder , with the help of hysterical media coverage , can destroy the tourism industry of a country for quite a while , as it do in Bali and in Turkey .
but the real fear come from the undisputed fact that no defense and no preventive measure can succeed against a determined suicide murderer .
this have not yet penetrate the thinking of the Western World .
the U.S. and Europe be constantly improve they defense against the last murder , not the next one .
we may arrange for the good airport security in the world .
but if you want to murder by suicide , you do not have to board a plane in order to explode yourself and kill many people .
who could stop a suicide murder in the midst of the crowded line wait to be check by the airport metal detector ?
how about the line to the check - in counter in a busy travel period ?
put a metal detector in front of every train station in Spain and the terrorist will get the bus .
protect the bus and they will explode in movie theater , concert hall , supermarket , shopping mall , school and hospital .
put guard in front of every concert hall and there will always be a line of people to be check by the guard and this line will be the target , not to speak of kill the guard themselves .
you can somewhat reduce you vulnerability by preventive and defensive measure and by strict border controls but not eliminate it and definitely not win the war in a defensive way .
and it be a war !
what be behind the suicide murder ?
money be , money and power and cold - blooded murderous incitement , nothing else .
it have nothing to do with true fanatic religious belief .
no Moslem preacher have ever blow himself up .
no son of a Arab politician or religious leader have ever blow himself up .
no relative of anyone influential have do it .
_ you expect some of the religious leader to do it themselves , or to talk they son into do it , if this be truly a supreme act of religious fervor ?
_ they interested in the benefit of go to Heaven ?
instead , they send outcast woman , naive child , retarded people and young incite hothead .
they promise they the delight , mostly sexual , of the next world , and pay they family handsomely after the supreme act be perform and enough innocent people be dead .
suicide murder also have nothing to do with poverty and despair .
the poor region in the world , by far , be Africa .
it never happen there .
there be numerous desperate people in the world , in different culture , country and continent .
desperation do not provide anyone with explosive , reconnaissance and transportation .
there be certainly more despair in _ Iraq than in Paul _ Iraq , and no one explode himself .
a suicide murder be simply a horrible , vicious weapon of cruel , inhuman , cynical , well - fund terrorist , with no regard to human life , include the life of they fellow countryman , but with very high regard to they own affluent well - being and they hunger for power .
the only way to fight this new " popular " weapon be identical to the only way in which you fight organized crime or pirate on the high seas : the offensive way .
like in the case of organized crime , it be crucial that the force on the offensive be united and it be crucial to reach the top of the crime pyramid .
you _ eliminate organized crime by arrest the little drug dealer on the street corner .
you must go after the head of the " family " .
if part of the public support it , other tolerate it , many be afraid of it and some try to explain it away by poverty or by a miserable childhood , organized crime will thrive and so will terrorism .
the United State understand this now , after September 11 .
Russia be begin to understand it .
Turkey understand it well .
I be very much afraid that most of Europe still do not understand it .
unfortunately , it seem that Europe will understand it only after suicide murder arrive in Europe in a big way .
in my humble opinion , this will definitely happen .
the Spanish train and the Istanbul bombing be only the beginning .
the unity of the civilized world in fight this horror be absolutely indispensable .
until Europe wake up , this unity will not be achieve .
* 2 . the second ingredient be word , more precisely lie . *
word can be lethal .
they kill people .
it be often say that politician , diplomat and perhaps also lawyer and business people must sometimes lie , as part of they professional life .
but the norm of politics and diplomacy be childish , in comparison with the level of incitement and total absolute deliberate fabrication , which have reach new height in the region we be talk about .
a incredible number of people in the Arab world believe that September 11 never happen , or be a American provocation or , even well , a Jewish plot .
you all remember the Iraqi Minister of Information , Mr. Mouhamad Said al - Sahaf and he press conference when the US force be already inside Baghdad .
disinformation at time of war be a accept tactic .
but to stand , day after day , and to make such preposterous statement , known to everybody to be lie , without even be ridicule in you own milieu , can only happen in this region .
Mr. Sahaf eventually become a popular icon as a court jester , but this do not stop some allegedly respectable newspaper from give he equal time .
it also do not prevent the western press from give credence , every day , even now , to similar liar .
after all , if you want to be a anti-Semite , there be subtle way of do it .
you do not have to claim that the holocaust never happen , and that the Jewish temple in Jerusalem never exist .
but million of Moslem be tell by they leader that this be the case .
when this same leader make other statement , the western media report they as if they could be true .
it be a daily occurrence that the same people who finance , arm and dispatch suicide murderer , condemn the act in English in front of western tv camera , talk to a world audience , which even partly believe they .
it be a daily routine to hear the same leader make opposite statement in Arabic to he people and in English to the rest of the world .
incitement by Arab tv , accompany by horror picture of mutilate body , have become a powerful weapon of that who lie , distort and want to destroy everything .
little child be raise on deep hatred and on admiration of so - call martyr , and the western world do not notice it because its own tv set be mostly tune to soap opera and game show .
I recommend to you , even though most of you do not understand Arabic , to watch Al Jazeera , from time to time .
you will not believe you own eye .
but word also work in other way , more subtle .
a demonstration in Berlin , carry banner support _ regime and feature three - year old baby dress as suicide murderer , be define by the press and by political leader as a " peace demonstration " .
you may support or oppose the Iraq war , but to refer to fan of Saddam , Arafat or Bin Laden as peace activist be a bit too much .
a woman walk into a Israeli restaurant in mid-day , eat , observe family with old people and child eat they lunch in the adjacent table and pay the bill .
she then blow herself up , kill 20 people , include many child , with head and arm roll around in the restaurant .
she be call " martyr " by several Arab leader and " activist " by the European press .
dignitary condemn the act but visit she bereaved family and the money flow .
there be a new game in town : the actual murderer be call " the military wing " , the one who pay he , equip he and send he be now call " the political wing " and the head of the operation be call the " spiritual leader " .
there be numerous other example of such orwellian nomenclature , use every day not only by terror chief but also by western media .
this word be much more dangerous than many people realize .
they provide a emotional infrastructure for atrocity .
it be Joseph Goebbels who say that if you repeat a lie often enough , people will believe it .
he be now be outperform by he successor .
* 3 . the third aspect be money . *
huge amount of money , which could have solve many social problem in this dysfunctional part of the world , be channel into three concentric sphere support death and murder .
in the inner circle be the terrorist themselves .
the money fund they travel , explosive , hideout and permanent search for soft vulnerable target .
the inner circle be primarily finance by terrorist state like Iran and Syria , until recently also by Iraq and Libya and early also by some of the communist regime .
this state , as well as the Palestinian Authority , be the safe haven of the wholesale murder vendor .
they be surround by a second wide circle of direct supporter , planner , commander , preacher , all of whom make a living , usually a very comfortable living , by serve as terror infrastructure .
finally , we find the third circle of so - call religious , educational and welfare organization , which actually do some good , feed the hungry and provide some schooling , but brainwash a new generation with hatred , lie and ignorance .
this circle operate mostly through mosque , madrasa and other religious establishment but also through incite electronic and print media .
it be this circle that make sure that woman remain inferior , that democracy be unthinkable and that exposure to the outside world be minimal .

overview
this conference will examine the business and regulatory challenge to U.S. electric system in transition in effectively expand transmission capacity to meet new demand in the large and more competitive regional market emerge under FERC 's RTO initiative .

we need to change the prod description for the lme product .

for Curr LME LME ( Spot ) 01 March 01 jpy / usd
a currency transaction with Enron Europe Finance & Trading Limited ( " EEFTL " ) as agent for Risk Management & Trading Corp. under which either ( a ) for the case in which counterparty submit a offer to buy from EEFTL , counterparty shall receive the base currency amount and shall pay the foreign currency amount , or ( b ) for the case in which counterparty submit a offer to sell to EEFTL , counterparty shall pay the base currency amount and shall receive the foreign currency amount .

the settlement date shall be the date ( s ) set forth in the product description on the website .

fyi
dear Justin
Marly ask I to respond to you .
as you know , the suffix online be purely descriptive and now use by many company .
therefore , any trade mark registration that incorporate the word online as a suffix in the way that you use it will not enable its owner to prevent other from use the word online .
give the above , if you have adequate protection for the word ENRON ( which cover the service that you offer on - line as well as you core activity ) , _ say that another application for the word ENRON ONLINE be probably unnecessary .
however , if you use a particular logo for the on - line service , that should be register .
I hope the above be clear .
Jonathan Day

" Lindh , Frank ( Law ) " < frl3@pge.com >
12/21/2000 07:50 pm
confidential settlement document per CPUC rule 51
gas accord ii settlement participant :
attach be _ gas accord ii ( ga ii ) settlement proposal .
we believe it address many of the issue and concern you have raise in the workshop .
as a overview , this proposal : * maintain the basic gas accord structure in place today for the period 2003 to 2007 . *
* offer end user transportation rate for 2003 low for most customer than rate in effect today . *
* provide for vintage redwood path rate for core customer . *
* offer a 7.5 cent / dth rate to large customer while minimize rate change to other customer , minimize the incentive for this customer to seek to bypass local transmission charge and other CPUC - approve charge . *
* adopt guideline to improve reliability and help moderate price in gas commodity market , and identify the capital project need to meet this guideline over the course of the ga ii period ( 2003 - 2007 ) . *
* provide a high degree of rate stability , with a 3.5 % escalator to capture both inflation and the cost of need capital project .
the guarantee rate will be adjustable only for significant change in the cost of capital or increase cost due to governmental requirement or catastrophic event . *
* preserve a rate differential between the redwood and baja path , although somewhat less than the current differential . *
* propose a two - stage open season for firm transportation service begin in 2003 , with end user receive a first option on available capacity . *
* maintain the core aggregation program with some adjustment .
PG&E also anticipate that the core procurement incentive mechanism ( cpim ) will be similar to _ mechanism , but will reflect the somewhat large capacity holding need to meet anticipate increase in core demand and to meet a 1 - day in 10 - year cold weather event .

probe the ' palace coup '
electricity : a panel focus on price hike and the action of the ISO president .
September 26 , 2001
by KIMBERLY KINDY
the Orange County Register
SACRAMENTO
a state Senate committee be set today to start serve 16 subpoena on electricity producer and official who manage _ energy grid to determine whether they act in concert to manipulate energy price .
the investigative committee , head by state Sen. Joe Dunn , D - Santa Ana , be focus on a series of event last fall fill with enough Shakespearean plot twist and intrigue that it have earn a name around the Capitol : " the palace coup . "
lawmaker and consumer group allege that the event - direct by the man who head the _ energy grid - fuel the California energy crisis , push the state into the power - buy business and help make billion of dollar for power producer .
the central question behind the palace coup be whether Terry Winter , the president of the Independent System Operator , act alone when he take step to remove key price cap design to limit the amount power generator could charge .
Winter defy he own board and Gov. Gray Davis when he file a 50 - page request to remove the cap , record and interview show .
" I _ know how this event could have take place without some concerted effort , " say Dunn .
the subpoena will force that involve , include Winter , to provide swear testimony about the event to the committee , and to turn over e-mail , personal calendar and memo .
Davis spokesman Steve Maviglio say the governor feel " betrayed " by the action of Winter .
" the governor believe it be the define moment , when what be a mount problem turn into a instant crisis , " Maviglio say .
Winter refuse comment , refer all question to the public relation office .
ISO spokesman Gregg Fishman say _ committee will find no criminal conduct .
the decision be make by ISO upper management with one goal in mind : to keep the light on .
at the time , generator be refuse to sell power in California because of the price cap .
" it be a emergency , " Fishman say .
" we have to take action . ''
what become known as the palace coup begin on October 26 when ISO board member vote for severe restriction on the amount of money electricity producer could charge for power .
the restriction would drive price as low as $ 65 per megawatt - nearly 12 time below the $ 750 per megawatt limit of seven month early .
" they ( electricity generator ) grin and bear the $ 750 price cap , but this new plan by ISO be too much , " say Dunn , whose committee have be investigate since March .
" all hell break loose . ''
record show that on October 31 , power generator and electricity trader file letter with the Federal Energy Regulatory Commission , demand that the new plan be kill .
the letter , six in all , be send within two hour of each other and represent dozen of power generator .
" if not remove immediately , the ( ISO ) price cap will sow confusion in the market , threaten reliability and stifle new investment in generating capacity , '' read one letter write by Duke Energy vice president William Hall iii .
although there be nothing illegal about the generator act together to lobby against price cap , Dunn believe the letter and other action around the same time show clear coordination among energy official .
he say the main aim of the subpoena will be to determine whether collusion occur to " fix " price , which would violate federal trade law .
in the October 31 letter , electricity producer tell federal official that if price cap _ remove it would lead to a collapse of the energy market .
the generator get they way .
the next day , the federal commission kill the new pricing plan .
what be leave in place be a $ 250 price cap establish five month early .
power producer then turn they attention toward kill that cap , say they _ make a profit even under this constraint .
they begin to withhold power from California , and on December 7 the ISO declare its first stage 3 emergency and brace for blackout , which be narrowly avert .
what follow the next day be consider by the governor and Dunn to be the pivotal moment of the energy crisis .
Winter , who in he position as president and chief operate officer of the ISO , submit a 50 - page emergency request , ask federal official to abolish the $ 250 price cap .
final authority over lift the cap rest with the federal government .
neither the ISO board , which have establish the price cap , nor the governor learn of _ action until the cap have be remove .
in fact , the attorney who help draft the emergency request , Charles Robinson , be in a meeting with representative of the governor and ISO board member just hour before the filing be make .
he _ mention anything about it .
" in retrospect , we should have tell they , '' Robinson say .
with the price cap gone , the generator file paperwork with federal regulator justify high cost .
" the ISO staff sit in a meeting with the _ key energy adviser with poker face , not say a word about something that be go on at the exact same moment , '' Maviglio say .
" it be beyond belief that they fail to mention something so significant .
this action accelerate the _ move toward bankruptcy and force the governor to move the state into the power - buy business . "
price for electricity jump from a average of $ 249 a megawatt to $ 700 a megawatt within three day , ISO record show .
Dunn believe the result overcharge for electricity exceed $ 30 billion .
Robinson say the filing - grant two hour after the request - help rather than hurt Californian .
price , he say , do not spike as a result .
instead they follow the skyrocket price of natural gas - which be use to run power plant to generate electricity .
Robinson say the emergency order allow the ISO to secure refund should overcharge for electricity be prove to federal official .
" we believe the action we take address a severe concern , '' Robinson say .
" in we view , we do not believe we change or make bad the financial situation .
we feel we make it good because it introduce a process for review and refund . "
Jan Smutney - Jones , who be the ISO board chairman at the time and executive director of a group that represent power generator , say Winter do not consult he about eliminate the price cap .
Smutney - Jones also say he be unaware of anyone in the power - generating community be consult .
" Terry do this by himself , '' say Smutney - Jones , executive director of the Independent Energy Producer .
" he do what he think have to be do at the time to keep the power flow . "
the ISO board call a emergency meeting the next week demand Winter explain he action .
some board member push to have Winter remove , but there be concern such action would lead to more chaos , the _ spokesman Maviglio say .
James J. Hoecker , the former Federal Energy Regulatory Commission chairman , defend make the December decision and also defend Winter .
" they file a emergency motion , and we be not about to let California go dark , '' Hoecker say .
" they ( ISO management ) do what any independent system operator would do . "
what _ committee hope to learn be why all this event transpire .
he believe memo and e-mail around the time of _ December 8 action should provide vital clue .
" we _ know why he do what he do , but we be eager to find out , " Dunn say .
" Terry say he make that filing in the interest of Californian , but I find that argument have no basis in fact . ''

the dance

Quebecker win U.S. bravery award
Pittsburgh -
a Quebec man be award a Carnegie Medal for bravery on Monday for save two friend by fight off a polar bear with a pocket knife two year ago on Baffin Island
Dr. Eric Fortier , 34 , of Gatineau , Que. , use a pocket knife to attack a polar bear on Baffin Island , just south of the Arctic Circle , to save two friend who be be maul .
" all of the research and all of the preparation I do lead up to the trip give no indication that there be bear in the Soper [ River ] valley where we be canoe , " Dr. Fortier say .
Dr. Fortier , a orthodontist , learn there be at least one polar bear in the central region of Baffin Island in July 2001 when he feel what he think be a dog lean on he tent wall .
" my first thought be to push it away , " he say .
" a few seconds late my girlfriend see the shadow of a _ paw through the tent fly and then it start rip through the ceiling . "
the polar bear be more dangerous than most other bear .
the latter usually consider human being a threat but the polar bear consider human a snack , expert say .
the two scream to frighten the bear and warn they friend in a tent several metre away but the bear rip into that tent and begin maul 31 - year - old Alain Parenteau .
" they scream change , " Dr. Fortier say .
" I grab my glass and my knife and unzip my tent and head out . "
the bear dwarf the 6 - foot - 1 Mr. Parenteau , knock he to the ground , he say .
Dr. Fortier throw a large rock at the bear , distract it and allow Parenteau to escape but it then turn on 25 - year - old Patricia Doyon , who be in the same tent .
again Dr. Fortier throw rock at the bear and again its target be able to escape .
" the bear give chase and I give chase , " he say .
" at some point , Patricia trip or the bear trip she and be at she back .
I be beside the _ head and I stab it with a upper cut below the jaw in the neck a couple of time . "
the bear run off .
while there be some fur and blood on the nine - centimetre blade , Dr. Fortier say he _ think he hurt the bear badly .
both Mr. Parenteau and Ms. Doyon , however , be bleed badly .
Dr. Fortier and he girlfriend lash two canoe together and paddle eight kilometre along the Soper River .
Dr. Fortier travel another three kilometre by foot to seek help in the near settlement .
both Mr. Parenteau and Ms. Doyon be airlift to a hospital and survive , though Mr. Parenteau have a gash within a centimetre of he jugular , Dr. Fortier say .
Dr. Fortier be one of 15 people to receive the Carnegie Medal on Monday .
the bronze medal be give to people who " risk they life to a extraordinary degree while save or attempt to save the life of other . "
the other Canadian recipient of the medal be Ronald Joseph Crawford , 42 , of Hamilton , who be kill August 4 , 2002 , while try to defend a Hamilton sandwich shop owner from a robber wield a knife .
Mr. Crawford throw several punch at the assailant before he be stab in the heart .
U.S. industrialist Andrew Carnegie start a hero fund in 1904 after be inspire by rescue story from a mine disaster that kill 181 people .
the award come with a $ 3500 ( U.S. ) grant .

when Sabeer Bhatia come up with the business plan for the mail service , he try all kind of name end in ' mail ' and finally settle for hotmail as it include the letter " html " - the programming language use to write web page .
it be initially refer to as HoTMaiL with selective uppercasing .
Hewlett Packard
Bill Hewlett and Dave Packard toss a coin to decide whether the company they found would be call Hewlett - Packard or Packard - Hewlett .
Intel
Bob Noyce and Gordon Moore want to name they new company ' Moore Noyce ' but that be already trademark by a hotel chain so they have to settle for a acronym of integrated electronics .

Mitch Kapor get the name for he company from ' the lotus position ' or ' padmasana ' .
Kapor use to be a teacher of Transcendental Meditation of Maharishi Mahesh Yogi .
Microsoft
coin by Bill Gates to represent the company that be devoted to microcomputer software .
originally christen Micro - Soft , the ' - ' be remove late on .
Motorola
founder Paul Galvin come up with this name when he company start manufacture radio for car .
the popular radio company at the time be call Victrola .
ORACLE
Larry Ellison and Bob Oats be work on a consulting project for the CIA ( Central Intelligence Agency ) .
the code name for the project be call Oracle ( the CIA see this as the system to give answer to all question or something such ) .
the project be design to help use the newly write sql code by IBM .
the project eventually be terminate but Larry and Bob decide to finish what they start and bring it to the world .
they keep the name Oracle and create the RDBMS engine .
late they keep the same name for the company .
Sony
it originate from the Latin word ' sonus ' mean sound , and ' sonny ' a slang use by American to refer to a bright youngster .

found by 4 Stanford University buddy , SUN be the acronym for Stanford University Network .

hello yheggy - ga ,
on September 21 , 2004 , the U.S. Senate Appropriations Committee approve $ 16.379 billion in funding for NASA for fiscal year 2005 .
this be a $ 200 million increase over what NASA receive for fiscal year 2004 .
U.S. Senate Committee on Appropriations
press release
September 21 , 2004
" National Aeronautics and Space Administration ( NASA ) : be fund at $ 16.379 billion , a increase of $ 200 million over the fy04 enact level , and a reduction of $ 665 million from the budget request .
a additional $ 800 million in emergency funding be add for NASA during the _ consideration of the bill .
-- the return to flight activity for the shuttle program be fund at $ 4.319 billion , the request level from the administration .
-- the International Space Station be fund at $ 1.6 billion .
the bill reduce ISS operation by $ 120 million due to the continue reduce capability of the ISS for at least half of fy05 .
-- the Moon / Mars vision :
--- the Crew Exploration Vehicle ( CEV ) be fund at $ 268 million .
--- a lunar exploration mission be fund at $ 20 million .
--- $ 10 million be provide for Centennial Challenge .
Neighborhood Reinvestment Corporation ( NRC ) : be fund at $ 115 million , the same as fy04 and the budget request . "

by Richard Spencer
( file : 19/11/2004 )
_ insatiable demand for energy be prompt fear of financial and diplomatic collision around the globe as it seek reliable supplies of oil from as far away as Brazil and Sudan .
a intrusion into Japanese territorial water by a Chinese nuclear submarine last week and a trade deal with Brazil be the late apparently unconnected consequence of _ soar economic growth .
increase car usage in China be create a high demand for petrol
the connection , however , lie in a order issue last year by President Hu Jintao to seek secure oil supplies abroad - preferably one which could not be stop by America in case of conflict over Taiwan .
the submarine incident be put down to a " technical error " by the Chinese government , which apologise to Japan .
but even before the incident the _ Daily , the government mouthpiece , have comment that competition over the East China Sea between the two country be " only a prelude of the game between China and Japan in the arena of international energy " .
the Brazil trade deal include funding for a joint oil - drilling and pipeline programme at a cost that expert say would add up to three time the cost of simply buy oil on the market .
the west , however , have pay little attention to this development .
for the United State and Europe be far more concerned with the even more sensitive issue of _ relation with " pariah state " .
in September , China threaten to veto any move to impose sanction on Sudan over the atrocity in Darfur .
it have invest $ 3 billion in the African _ oil industry , which supply it with seven per cent of its need .
then , this month , it say that it oppose move to refer _ nuclear stand - off with the International Atomic Energy Agency to the United Nation Security Council .
a week before , _ second big state oil firm have sign a $ 70 billion deal for oilfield and natural gas development with Iran , which already supply 13 per cent of _ need .
China have its own reserve of oil and natural gas and once be a net oil exporter .
but as its economy have expand by a average of nine per cent per year for the last two decade , so have its demand for energy .
this year it overtake Japan as the _ second large consumer of energy , behind the US .
its project demand , boost by a huge rise in car ownership as well as the need to find alternative to pollute coal for electricity generation , have contribute to the surge in the price of oil this year .
shortage be already lead to power cut in the big city .
since President Hu order state - own oil firm to " go abroad " to ensure supply , they have begin drill for gas in the East China Sea , just west of the line that Japan regard as its border .
Japan protest , to no avail , that the project should be a joint one .
the two be also set to clash over _ oil wealth .
China be furious that Japan have outbid it in they battle to determine the route of the pipeline that Russia intend to build to the Far East .
Japan favour a route to the sea , enable oil to be ship to both Japan and China .
China want a overland route through its own territory , which would give it ultimate control if hostility break out .
increasingly , analyst be say that _ effort have go beyond what be safe or even in its own interest .
Claude Mandil , the executive director of the International Energy Agency in Paris , say the reserve in the East China Sea be hardly worth the trouble .
" nobody think that there will be a lot of oil and gas in this part of the world , " he say .
" it may be a difficult political issue but I _ think the energy content be worthwhile . "
Eurasia Group , a New York - base firm of political analyst , say its oil expert work out that China be pay such a inflate price for its investment in Brazil that the cost for the oil it end up with be three time the market price .
" if _ economy falter , which , in my view , appear increasingly likely , then commodity price will plummet , and with they , the value of the asset that produce they , " Jason Kindopp , _ lead China analyst , say .
" Beijing may end up in a early 1990 Japan situation , where it be force to sell recently purchase overseas asset for a fraction of what it pay for they . "
_ wide aggression to secure oil and gas be the great threat to its international standing in the next decade .
" Sudan be the primary example , " he say .
" it mark the first time in recent year that China have promise to wield its veto power in the UN Security Council against a petition initiate by the United State and back by France and Great Britain . "

visualization as a helpful begin technique
-----------------------------------------------
if you consider that you still need the assistance of other visualization to help the mind feel the spirit of transcendence , try the follow before move onto the more formal method below .
visualisation can be as useful tool , but meditation be more than that .
meditation have to do with what be call ideation .
it be always good to stick to a formal intense meditation practice like the one for beginner describe in the mp3 file that follow after the visualisation .
find a comfortable place on the floor and sit with you leg cross .
place you hand one on top of the other in you lap , keep you back straight , eye close and tongue on the roof of you mouth .
you breathing should be calm and relaxed , through the nose .
spend a minute or so concentrate on you breath , feel the air flow through you nostril .
1 . warm sun visualization
continue to breathe slowly and deeply .
with each breath , feel the muscle in you body become light and light , and also you external motor and sensory organ be feel like they be withdraw from the world into a special inner quietness .
imagine the tension melt away as you continue breathe rhythmically and naturally .
picture yourself sit on a warm , tropical beach bask in the glow of the sun ... .
visualize the vivid , beautiful colour of the earth ( its flower and plant ) , the sea next to you , and the sky above you .
feel yourself float above the earth and sea .
as you sit above the world , the warmth of the golden sun penetrate you body and make you feel warm and warm .
it surround you .
the golden ray feel soft and soothing .
now you be far above the earth - into space .
everything around you be so vast .
yet , there be warmth and a familiarity with the vastness .
you want to merge you mind with the great universal mind that surround you .
continue to ideate on this intense desire for you mind to merge with the that universal consciousness .
and while do so continue use the baba nam kevalam mantra ( breathe in with baba nam , breathe out with kevalam ) .
try this for 5 to 10 minute .
now come back to earth again - slowly .
imagine yourself sit on the beach serenely and restfully .
you muscle be loose and limp .
feel you body sink slightly into the sand make that earthly connection again .
the _ ray and warmth be still with you , surround you .
you be in a state of peace and relaxation .
with each breath , watch you body and ensure that it remain relaxed - at peace .
continue to feel the warmth of the sunlight all over you body , warm you deeply and gently .
you want to bring something back with you from you deep space experience where you sense you mind merge with the universal mind .
this will be the warmth of the sun - a close reminder and link between earth and the infinite space .
visualize the inside of you body bath in the golden light , absorb every ray and glow as radiantly as the sun .
a warm , gentle breeze swirl around you body and relax you even more .
let you mind and body be totally at peace .
now feel yourself return to where you sit ... move you hand and foot a little , stretch they .
open you eye .
2 . mountain visualization
another thing you can try .
imagine _ sit on top of a mountain , and that _ the most peaceful place you can think of .
feel that _ sit there in complete peace , right on top of the world .
now imagine that infinite happiness be surround you in every direction .
feel _ completely surround by that infinite peace and happiness .
now start to repeat within you mind the mantra : baba nam kevalam .
its meaning be " infinite happiness be everywhere " .
feel the meaning , _ just think of its wordy meaning or try to translate from Sanskrit ( baba nam kevalam ) to a English meaning ( infinite peace and happiness ) .
think internally , intuitively , not by word , of the meaning , as _ repeat it .
this be call ideation .
it be important to take the idea , not just the intellectual analysis .
touch deep into the idea be what build intuition - it be a synthetic process .
whereas , try to translate and grapple with wordy meaning be a intellectual mechanism - a analytical process .
feel _ surround by infinite peace and happiness , and feel that you own sense of existence be in direct contact with that endless peace and happiness all around you .
you can go far and feel that you unit consciousness , a dot in the infinite consciousness , be merge with infinity .
continue for as long as you like , then open you eye .
ok that be fairly basic :) .
the important point be to develop some psycho-spiritual connection between you mind and the universal consciousness or supreme consciousness .
_ worry if you have trouble concentrate on the mantra and ideation - _ normal .
it take some time and practice to be able to focus on the one thought .
the main thing be to keep practice .
if you _ practice , then nothing happen .
well maybe a miracle could happen , but _ face it _ ordinary people and so require practical day to day technique !

one of " _ " major effort be to collect signature for the attach " declaration of religious leader , " which have be and will again be present to member of the NC legislature .
it present the case for marriage equality and state , " we be resolve that the State should not interfere with same - gender couple who choose to marry and share fully and equally in the rights , responsibility , and commitment of civil marriage . "
a measure to amend the NC constitution to ban gay marriage be defeat last year but already have be reintroduce in the 2005 legislative session , so there be a real need for visible support for the " pro-same - gender - marriage " side of this issue .

North Carolina Religious Coalition for Marriage Equality declaration of religious leader April 19 , 2004
the most fundamental human right , after the necessity of food , clothing and shelter , be the right to affection and the supportive love of other human being .
we become most fully human when we love another person .
we can grow in we capacity to be human - to be loving - in a family unit .
this right to love and form a family be so fundamental that we United State Constitution take it for grant in its dedication to " secure the blessing of liberty to ourselves and we posterity . "
the North Carolina Constitution likewise affirm the " inalienable rights " of human being to " life , liberty , the enjoyment of the fruit of they own labor , and the pursuit of happiness . "
throughout history , tyrant have know that by deny the right of oppress people to form and nurture family , they can kill the spirit of that people .
> from the shameful history of slavery in America , the injustice of forbid people to marry be evident as a denial of a basic human right .
the American law forbid interracial marriage , now strike down , be clearly discriminatory .
denial of the status of marriage to that who would freely accept its responsibility create legal and economic inequity and social injustice .
we feel call to protest and oppose this injustice .
as religious people , clergy and lay leader , we be mandate by faith to stand for justice in we common civic life .
we oppose the use of sacred text and religious tradition to deny legal equity to same - gender couple .
as concerned citizen we affirm the liberty of adult of the same gender to love and marry .
we insist that no one , especially the state , be allow to coerce people into marriage or bar two consent adult , whether of the same or differ gender , from form the family unit that let they be more fully loving , thus more fully human .
we respect the fact that debate and discussion continue in many of we religious community as to the scriptural , theological and liturgical issue involve .
however , we draw on we many faith tradition to arrive at a common conviction .
we be resolve that the state should not interfere with same - gender couple who choose to marry and share fully and equally in the rights , responsibility , and commitment of civil marriage .
we affirm freedom of conscience in this matter .
we recognize that the state may not require religious group to officiate at , or bless , same - gender marriage .
likewise , a denial of state civil recognition dishonor the religious conviction of that community and clergy who officiate at , and bless , same - gender marriage .
the state may not favor the conviction of one religious group over another by deny individual they fundamental right to marry and to have that marriage recognize by civil law .
as faith leader , we commit ourselves to public action , visibility , education , and mutual support in the service of the right and freedom to marry .
--
Tom Dempsey Gulf Breeze , FL 850-748-0740

the one reason why all American should oppose the nomination of Samuel Alito
he would tear down we system of check and balance , give far too much power to the President
my fellow American :
as many of you may have hear , President Bush have nominate a long - time federal judge name Samuel Alito to become the next member of the United State Supreme Court , to fill a vacancy create by the retirement of another member of the court .
under we constitution , this nomination _ take effect unless and until the United State Senate give its consent , as describe in we constitution , article ii , section 2 .
a copy of the constitution , with link back to the official source , be locate at http://loveallpeople.org/usconstitutiona.txt
judge Samuel Alito be very highly qualified by all of the normal standard use to evaluate candidate for this position :
he have a very high intellect .
he graduate very high in he class , from Princeton undergraduate and from law school at Yale .
he have a long and distinguished record , include many year as a federal appeal judge , the next level below Supreme Court .
he have encyclopedic knowledge of hundred of different Supreme Court case , and he can recite detail from memory .
he demonstrate a excellent " judicial temperament , " be courteous , mild - mannered , respectful of all people ; careful in he work , meticulous in detail .
he co-worker love he .
he fellow judge love he .
he family love he .
President Bush love he .
yes , it be true that some people _ like the way they think he will vote on the Supreme Court .
but other people do like the way they think he will vote , and the one who favor he seem to outnumber the one who oppose he .
so now the Senate be get ready to vote soon , on whether to approve he or not ; and at this moment ( evening of January 27 , 2006 ) it look like he have more than the fifty - one vote need for approval .
the President be very eager to go ahead quickly and get this vote , because he very much want to have Samuel Alito on the Supreme Court , to be judge the case Bush be interested in .
so there be a lot of hurry - up pressure on the Senate to give its prompt vote of approval .
there be a old saying that apply in this situation : " act in haste , repent at leisure . "
sometimes you can make a bad decision very quickly , then regret it for many year to come .
that be what be about to happen with judge Samuel Alito , in my opinion , because he have one tragic flaw - a very serious blind spot in he thinking - which make he completely unacceptable for the position of Supreme Court justice : he do not really agree with the system of " check and balance " build into the constitution , and he be ready to start tear it down in order to follow the " Unitary Executive Theory , " which call for vastly - increase presidential power at the expense of Congress and the Supreme Court .
and because of this tragic flaw . . .
" he would tear down we system of check and balance , give far too much power to the President . "
in we constitutional system , we have three branch of the Federal Government : the legislative , executive , and judicial branch .
and the basic idea behind the check and balance we have be that if one branch of the government go crazy , the other two can hold it down .
but Samuel Alito believe in a little - know constitutional theory - call the " Unitary Executive Theory " - which say that the President should have complete control over the executive branch , and that the executive branch should be in charge of almost everything that the government actually do , include the function of the independent agency which be design to be free of presidential control , and the military , which exist , which be regulate , and which be fund by specific authority give by the constitution to Congress , not to the President .
the military be not part of the executive branch : it be a separate entity .
" Commander in Chief " _ mean that he be the boss of the military , merely that he be the administrator , just as he be the administrator of the executive branch , charge with " execute faithfully " all the law pass by Congress and all the decision render by the Supreme Court .
under the Unitary Executive Theory , the law of Congress and decision of the Supreme Court have no actual authority unless the President agree with they .
and so Congress and the Supreme Court become mere advisor to the President , with no real authority over he .
and the President become a dictator , unrestrained by anything in the constitution , back up by the armed force , which would be entirely under he personal control .
and thus the United State of America - the land of the free and the home of the brave - become just another military dictatorship , no good than Nazi Germany or fascist Italy during World War ii .
and that be why all American should oppose the nomination of Samuel Alito .
for detail and further proof , please see this website :
testimony at http://judiciary.senate.gov/testimony.cfm?id=1725&wit_id=4905
description and link at http://www.unitaryexecutive.net
blessing to you .
may God help we all .
and may God bless America !
Rev. Bill McGinnis , director http://www.loveallpeople.org and http://www.internetchurchofchrist.org

China launch its second manned spaceflight mission
secretive effort keep outsider in the dark about the _ goal
by MARK CARREAU
copyright 2005 Houston Chronicle
Reuters
China launch Shenzhou VI , its second manned spacecraft , early today in northwest _ Gansu Province .
a pair of military pilot embark on _ second manned space flight early today , hurtle into orbit on a test mission that could span five day .
the crew of the Shenzhou VI spacecraft be identify as Fei Junlong , 40 , and Nie Haishen , 41 , by _ official news agency .
the successful launch from the Jiuquan Satellite Launch Center in northwest China follow the solo flight of Yang Liwei in October 2003 .
he one - day mission vault he communist homeland into the elite circle of spacefaring nation - Russia and the United State - that can launch and sustain human in space .
most expert believe China intend to develop a small space station of its own over the next several year .
but they remain uncertain about whether China aim to beat the United State to the moon in its secretive space effort .
President Bush have direct NASA to return to the moon by 2018 with a new generation of human explorer .
_ " be not a fly - by - night program , " say Joan Johnson - Freese , a expert on national security who follow space development in the Asian nation at the Naval War College in Newport , R.I .
" they be not in any hurry .
they want a program that will be a success , " Johnson - Freese say .
" they be not go to rush it , because they _ want it to be a budget buster .
economics will be a big determiner in the speed of they program . "
_ overture to join the U.S. - lead effort to develop the 16 - nation international space station have be thwart for more than a decade over a range of issue , include the Asian _ human rights policy and worry it could acquire technology that could pose a security threat .
the freeze thaw some after _ 2003 mission .
China be among 30 nation invite to send a delegate to NASA - sponsor roundtable discussion on _ strategy to reach the moon with astronaut as the first step in the exploration of Mars and other - deep space destination .
" we applaud _ space achievement , " NASA spokesman Allard Beutel say Tuesday .
" we wish they a successful return of they astronaut . "
he stress , however , that NASA would not follow this _ Chinese mission through formal channel .
at present , there be no plan for additional meeting with foreign power to discuss the Bush exploration initiative or to extend a invitation to China to join the space station partnership , Beutel say .
the flight of Fei and Nie could mark the end of the open chapter in a three - phase Chinese space initiative , Johnson - Freese say .
the first phase , she say , will demonstrate the capability of a multi-compartment spacecraft that will leave a test module in orbit when the two flier return to Earth .
the Chinese _ second phase will include spacewalk on future mission and demonstration of docking and undocking technique .
the final phase will feature the assembly and operation of a long - duration space lab .
at least one expert believe _ intention might include a surprise attempt to circle the moon with astronaut before _ plan lunar return .
" the American would be wise to plan accordingly , " say John E. Pike , director of the Alexandria , Va. - base globalsecurity.org , a small national security think tank .
" there be always the possibility they could jam we up , make we look like we be not numero uno , " Pike say .
during the U.S. and Russian lunar race during the Cold War , NASA score a early coup by circle the moon with the Apollo 8 crew over the 1968 Christmas holiday .
as it turn out , the Soviet never make it to the moon .
" ( China ) could be the second country to do that , " Pike say .
" they would get in line in front of the Russian .
and they would not have to land on the moon to take we down a notch . "
_ concern be base on _ development of a new medium - lift rocket , the Long March V , and the construction of a new space launch complex on Hainan Island in the South China Sea .
the two development , he say , could eventually enable _ space program to mature to the point that expert could assemble and launch from _ orbit a spacecraft capable of circle the moon with astronaut and return home .

Blue Planet : _ afraid of Big Bad Wolf ?
by Dan Whipple
UNITED PRESS INTERNATIONAL
Boulder , CO , February 23 ( UPI ) --
ever since he eat up Red Riding _ grandma and blow down the house of two - third of the Three Little Pig , the Big Bad Wolf have hold a persistently bad reputation .
in part because of that reputation , the gray wolf be nearly exterminate from the low 48 state by the 1920 , except for a small remnant population on Isle Royale National Park in _ Lake Superior .
the last wolf be kill in Yellowstone National Park in 1943 .
western sheep and cattle rancher , on whose behalf this extermination campaign be conduct , gratefully dust they hand of the wolf and write he off as a job well do .
they sheep could graze , they cow could ruminate and never a discouraging word would be hear .
after the major kill - off , wolf outside of Alaska and Canada exist mostly as legend .
like ufo or Sasquatch , several people claim to see fleeting lone wolf , usually in Yellowstone .
in the 1960 , a group shoot a movie in the Wyoming park reportedly import some captive wolf , then release they when they shooting be done .
if so , this happy band have not be hear from since .
rumor also have it some renegade biologist bring a cage pair to Yellowstone and release they into the wild sometime in the 1970 , hope to reestablish a breed population .
if true , the caper fail .
over time , the _ absence seem to rehabilitate its image .
eventually , a trickle of support appear for bring the predator back to its former home range in the northern Rocky Mountain .
this trickle grow into a flood , result in 14 wolf be reintroduce in Yellowstone in 1995 by the U.S. Fish and Wildlife Service -- albeit over the strong and still - continue objection of rancher .
this wolf pack have flourish , and now there be a estimate 850 wolf roam the northern Rocky , where merely 10 year ago there be none .
one compelling argument for reintroduction be the wolf act as a keystone predator , a animal that affect the population , behavior and ecology of a wide variety of species within its range .
some recent research conduct by Oregon State University have give considerable credence to this idea .
OSU forestry professor William Ripple and Robert Beschta have find that wolf actually promote stream - bank stabilization , although they have give the phenomenon the unfortunate name of " the ecology of fear " -- something that smack of the horrible pr result from the _ relationship with Riding Hood and the Three Pig .
they explain that elk in Yellowstone use to browse unmolested on young aspen and willow grow near the bank of stream , a behavior that prevent the sapling from reach mature stage and increase the possibility of soil erosion .
since reintroduction , however , Ripple and Beschta have find , fear of the wolf apparently have discourage the elk from spend too much time at stream bank -- where they be out in the open -- and munch on the sapling .
" all you have to do be look at the photograph , " Ed Bangs , wolf recovery coordinator for the U.S. Fish and Wildlife Service , tell _ Blue Planet ,
" you say , ' wow ! '
a area that use to be bald as a billiard ball be now a sea of willow . "
this simple change have trigger a veritable ecological cascade in Yellowstone .
more streamside willow and aspen have mean good habitat for beaver , for instance .
where there have be only one beaver colony in the _ northern range before the wolf return , now there be nine .
" it may be uninteresting to a lot of people , " Beschta tell Blue Planet .
" _ a lot of impact on plant and they say , ' who care ? '
but _ be look at streamside community .
since wolf recovery , streamside plant , willow and cottonwood provide food for other critter -- beaver , a whole variety of avian species , berry - produce shrub that bear can use .
_ important with regard to the quality of stream .
the plant provide shade and root strength for bank stability .
plant be critical to wildland ecosystem . "
Yellowstone have a vast elk herd , one of the large in the world .
Bangs say although the number of elk have not decline very much since the wolf come back , they behavior appear markedly different .
" _ pretty suspicious of make broad generalization , " however , he caution .
" wolf be still pretty new .
_ only be there for 10 year .
in 10 more year _ have a good idea . "
wolf reintroduction in the northern Rocky have be so successful the Fish and Wildlife Service have move to reduce the _ status from endangered to threatened and , eventually , to remove it from the endangered species list altogether .
Bangs say the agency have establish viable wolf pack in the northern Rocky , as require by federal regulation .
some conservationist want the protection extend so wolf can move into other state , include Colorado , Utah and Oregon , among other .
on January 31 , Oregon Federal District Court Judge Robert E. Jones appear to agree with they .
he vacate the FWS decision to downgrade the _ status .
Bangs say he agency be still review the decision .
regardless of the _ legal status , its future expansion into new area now seem likely .
wolf can migrate considerable distance .
a Yellowstone wolf be find dead , hit by a car , on a Colorado highway last year , several hundred mile from home .
meanwhile , he reputation seem to be improve , although Bangs note a " pretty interesting social dynamic . "
there be only about 850 wolf in the west , but there be a estimate 31000 mountain lion .
pound for pound , mountain lion eat more game and more livestock than wolf .
they even occasionally attack people , which wolf do not -- despite the propaganda from the Brother Grimm .
yet people seem willing -- even eager -- to accommodate mountain lion , despite the risk .
it remain to be see whether they will extend the same courtesy to the arrive gray wolf .
regard that rumor about wolf live in Yellowstone prior to the official reintroduction ?
they seem to be just that : rumor .
true , there be about 300000 wolf and wolf hybrid keep as pet in the United State .
it also be likely people have release some of this animal into the wild hope they would survive -- for instance , a ranger in Glacier Park catch someone in this very act not long ago .
Bangs say this animal be not equip to survive in the wild , however , and they all almost certainly have die .
he say after 10 year of dna testing on northern Rocky wolf , scientist have not find a single strain that do not belong to one of the wolf the agency release -- or they descendant .
