climate : human fuss , animal adjust
by Dan Whipple
UNITED PRESS INTERNATIONAL
Boulder , CO , November 15 ( UPI ) --
scientist can argue all they want about how many degree Celsius -- or Fahrenheit -- the planet be warm and what the trend portend , but meanwhile _ plant , insect and animal be not wait for the outcome .
they already be alter they pattern of behavior in response to what be happen .
it turn out one of the sure barometer of the warm climate be the response of the non-human natural world to change condition , and biologist who study the response have be aware for some year the biosphere be acknowledge global warming .
Nina Leopold Bradley , a plant ecologist and daughter of the conservation pioneer Aldo Leopold , publish a 1999 paper in the Proceedings of the National Academy of Science on she 61 - year uninterrupted phenological record .
phenology study a _ development and life cycle -- the pulse of life .
_ record of 300 phenophase find that even prior to 1999 , spring be arrive in high latitudes several week early than in the early year of she data .
bird arrive soon on they migration from the south and plant flower early .
the eastern phoebe be show up about 20 day before it use to .
the forest phlox be bloom in late April instead of mid-May .
half of the 300 phenophase Leopold track show a response consistent with warming .
in England , the cuckoo return early .
a analysis of 65 bird species in the United Kingdom show about one - third be lay they egg four to seven day early than they do 25 year ago .
" one of the major , most well - document and robust finding in ecology over the past century have be the crucial role of climate in determine the geographical distribution of species and ecological community , " conclude a report title " observe Impact of Global Climate Change in the United State , " release by the Pew Center on Global Climate last week .
Pew researcher look at about 40 study that could provide a assessment of whether climate be affect biology .
" half of the study provide strong evidence of a causal link between the biological change and climate change , " say Camille Parmesan , a University of Texas - Austin biologist and one of the _ lead expert on this issue .
this change be occur across all species , Parmesan tell _ Climate .
" across the United State , the northern edge of _ range be expand , " she say .
Parmesan have spend much of she career study the checkerspot butterfly , which migrate between Mexico and southern California .
some localize extinction already have occur across some of its habitat .
" empirical research point to climate as be a strong driver , " she say .
" there have be large number of population extinction in Mexico and southern California in area where the habitat be still acceptable . "
accord to _ early study , one extinction event , for instance , be trigger when a checkerspot population migrate north prematurely , rely on a warm temperature signal , then be catch in a severe snowstorm in its northern habitat .
throughout the United State , she say , " spring be about two week early .
tree swallow be nest nine day early .
tropical species have move up to Florida and the Gulf Coast .
bird and butterfly watcher be see many , many new species come up from Mexico and the Caribbean . "
as the Pew report conclude , " sufficient study now exist to conclude that the consequence of climate change be already detectable within U.S. ecosystem . "
such consequence include shifting and , in some case , contraction of range and change in species composition within ecosystem .
the report also find alteration of ecosystem process such as carbon cycling and storage .
the alaskan tundra , for instance , have switch from be a net sink of carbon dioxide -- absorb and store more carbon from the atmosphere than it release -- to " be a net source of co2 ( release more carbon than be store ) because warm winter have allow dead plant matter previously store in the soil to decompose and release co2 . "
the Pew report coincide with the release in Iceland of the " Arctic Climate Impact Assessment . "
the ACIA -- with participation by the United State , Canada , Denmark , Finland , Iceland , Norway , the Russian Federation and Sweden -- be begin in 2000 .
" the impact of global warming be affect people now in the Arctic , " say ACIA chair Robert Corell .
" the Arctic be experience some of the most rapid and severe climate change on Earth .
the impact of climate change on the region and the globe be project to increase substantially in the year to come . "
the ACIA find arctic winter temperature have increase 4 degree to 7 degree Fahrenheit in the last 50 year and should go up about twice that much in the next 100 year .
arctic summer sea ice will decline by 50 percent by the end of the 21st century , the assessment find , with some model predict complete disappearance of summer sea ice .
" should the Arctic Ocean become ice - free in summer , it be likely that polar bear and some seal species would be drive toward extinction , " the report conclude .
as with so much climate research , not everyone agree with this dire prediction .
a third report , " the Impact of Climate Change : a Appraisal for the Future , " complete by the Britain - base International Policy Network and release almost simultaneously with the other two , fall somewhat into that category .
on the one hand , the IPN report agree " climate model generally predict that the temperature rise in the Arctic will substantially exceed the global rise .
this apply especially in the high Arctic where the ice cover be expect to diminish substantially with the effect that the surface absorption of solar radiation will greatly increase . "
on the other hand , the report think the news might not be so bad for the North Atlantic fishery .
" the impact of global warming on fish stock and fishery be hard to judge , " the IPN report say .
" a warming of the magnitude predict be more likely than not to be beneficial to the fishery of the North Atlantic . "
the important commercial species that probably would benefit from warming include cod , haddock , saithe , herring , blue whiting and several type of flatfish and crustacean -- such as the Norway lobster .
important species that probably would decline include shrimp , capelin , Greenland halibut and some variety of flatfish .
hide in this laundry list -- and in the pile of study examine by the Pew researcher -- be one of the fundamental chasm divide participant in the global warming debate .
the IPN report examine commercial fish species , but it neglect important non-commercial animal , such as seal and polar bear .
in a limited economic sense , therefore , the organization can argue warming might be a good thing .
the problem be whether one care what happen to the polar bear , checkerspot butterfly and other unconsumable .
the Pew researcher try to transcend the economic argument .
they assume a value -- unspecified -- for non-commercial species , and in do so render the warming news a bit less rosy .
this tug - of - war over calculate economic value be the one that ultimately will have to be decide by human , because animal and plant can adjust only so much .
" when dandelion have set the mark of May on Wisconsin pasture , it be time to listen for the final proof of spring , " write Aldo Leopold in " a Sand County Almanac . "
" sit down on a tussock , cock you ear at the sky , dial out the bedlam of meadowlark and redwing , and soon you may hear it : the flight of the upland plover , just now back from the Argentine . "
or maybe not .
--

attack on Iran : a loom folly
by William Rivers Pitt
truthout _ _ _ _ _ _ _ | perspective
Monday 09 January 2006
the wire have be hum since before the new year with report that the Bush administration be plan a attack on Iran .
" the Bush administration be prepare its NATO ally for a possible military strike against suspect nuclear site in Iran in the New Year , accord to German media report , reinforce similar early suggestion in the Turkish media , " report UPI on December 30th .
" the Berlin daily Der Tagesspiegel this week , " continue UPI , " quote ' NATO intelligence source ' who claim that the NATO ally have be inform that the United State be currently investigate all possibility of bring the mullah - lead regime into line , include military option .
this ' all option be open ' line have be President George W _ publicly state policy throughout the past 18 month . "
a examination of the ramification of such a attack be desperately in order .
1 . blowback in Iraq
the recent election in Iraq be dominate by a amalgam of religiously fundamentalist shi'ite organization , principally the Dawa Party and the Supreme Council for Islamic Revolution in Iraq ( SCIRI ) .
both Dawa and SCIRI have umbilical connection to the fundamentalist shi'ite leadership in Iran that go back decade .
in essence , Iran now own a significant portion of the Iraqi government .
should the United State undertake military action against Iran , the ramification in Iraq would be immediate and extreme .
in the first eight day of January , eighteen US troops have be kill in Iraq , compound by another twelve death from a Black Hawk helicopter crash on Saturday .
much of the violence aim at American force be come from disgruntled Sunni faction that have they own militia , believe the last election be a sham , and hold little political power in the government .
if the US attack Iran , it be probable that American force - already tax by attack from Sunni faction - will also face reprisal attack in Iraq from shi'ite faction loyal to Iran .
the result will be a dramatic escalation in US and civilian casualty , US force will be require to bunker themselves further into they basis , and US force will find themselves require to fight the very government they just finish help into power .
Iraq , already a seethe cauldron , will sink far into chaos .
2 . _ armament
unlike Iraq , Iran have not spend the last fifteen year have its conventional force wear down by grueling sanction , repeat attack , and two American - lead war .
while _ conventional army be not what it be during the heyday of the Iran - Iraq war - they armament have deteriorate and the veteran of that last war have retire - the nation enjoy substantial military strength nonetheless .
accord to a report issue by the Center for Strategic and International Study in December of 2004 , Iran " have some 540000 man under arm and over 350000 reserve .
they include 120000 Iranian Revolutionary Guard train for land and naval asymmetrical warfare .
_ military also include holding of 1613 main battle tank , 21600 other armored fighting vehicle , 3200 artillery weapon , 306 combat aircraft , 60 attack helicopter , 3 submarine , 59 surface combatant , and 10 amphibious ship . "
" Iran be now the only regional military power that pose a significant conventional military threat to Gulf stability , " continue the CSIS report .
" Iran have significant capability for asymmetric warfare , and pose the additional threat of proliferation .
there be considerable evidence that it be develop both a long - range missile force and a range of weapon of mass destruction .
it have never properly declare its holding of chemical weapon , and the status of its biological weapon program be unknown . "
a MILNET brief issue in February 2005 report , " due to its position astride the Persian Gulf , Iran have constantly be a threat to the gulf .
the so call ' tanker ' war in the late 1980 put Iran squarely in the bullseye of all nation seek to transport oil out of the region .
even the small navy that Iran put to sea be capable enough to harass shipping , and several case of small boat operation against oil well head in the gulf during that period make it clear small asymmetrical tactic of the Iranian navy could be quite effective . "
" more concerning , " continue the MILNET brief , " be the priority place on expand and modernize its navy .
the CSIS report cite numerous area where Iran have fund modernization include the most troublesome aspect , anti-shipping cruise missile : ' Iran have obtain new anti-ship missile and missile patrol craft from China , midget submarine from North Korea , submarine from Russia , and modern mine . ' "
it be _ missile armament that pose the great concern for American force in the gulf , especially for the US Navy .
_ coast face the Persian Gulf be a loom wall of mountain that look down upon any naval force array in that water .
the gulf itself only have one exit , the Strait of Hormuz , which be also dominate by the mountainous Iranian coastline .
in essence , Iran hold the high ground in the gulf .
missile battery array in that mountain could raise bloody havoc with any fleet deploy below .
of all the missile in _ armament , the most dangerous be the Russian - make SS - N - 22 Sunburn .
this missile be , simply , the fast anti-ship weapon on the planet .
the Sunburn can reach Mach 3 at high altitude .
its maximum low - altitude speed be mach 2.2 , some three time fast than the American - make Harpoon .
the Sunburn take two short minute to cover its full range .
the _ manufacturer state that one or two missile could cripple a destroyer , and five missile could sink a 20000 ton ship .
the Sunburn be also superior to the Exocet missile .
recall that it be two Exocet that rip the USS Stark to shred in 1987 , kill 37 sailor .
the Stark could not see they to stop they .
the US aircraft carrier Theodore Roosevelt be currently deploy in the Persian Gulf , with some 7000 soul aboard .
sail with the Roosevelt be the Tarawa Expeditionary Strike Force , which include the USS Tarawa , the USS Austin , and the USS Pearl Harbor .
the USS Austin be likewise deploy in the gulf .
the Sunburn missile , with its incredible speed and ability to avoid radar detection , would do terrible damage this ship if Iran choose to retaliate in the gulf after a American attack within its border .
beyond the naval threat be the possibility of Iran throw its military muscle into the ongoing struggle in Iraq .
currently , the US be face a asymmetrical attack from group wield small arm , shoulder - fire grenade and roadside bomb .
the vaunted American military have suffer 2210 death and ten of thousand of wounded from this form of warfare .
the occupation of Iraq have become a guerrilla war , a siege that have last more than a thousand day .
if Iran decide to throw any or all of its 23000 armored fighting vehicle , along with any or all of its nearly million - strong army , into the Iraq fray , the situation in the Middle East could become unspeakably dire .
3 . the Syrian connection
in February of 2005 , Iran and Syria agree upon a mutual protection pact to combat " challenge and threat " in the region .
this be a specific reaction to the American invasion of Iraq , and a reaction to _ condemnation of Syria after the death of Lebanese Prime Minister Rafik Hariri , which be widely see as a assassination order from Damascus .
a attack on Iran would trigger this mutual defense pact , and could conceivably bring Syria into direct conflict with American force .
like Iran , _ military be nothing to scoff at .
virtually every credible analysis have Syria stand as the strong military force in the Middle East after Israel .
Damascus have be intent for year upon establish significant military strength to serve as a counterweight to _ overwhelming capability .
as of 2002 , Syria have some 215000 soldier under arm , 4700 tank , and a massive artillery capability .
the Syrian Air Force be comprise of ten to eleven fighter / attack squadron and sixteen fighter squadron , total somewhere near 650 aircraft .
Syria also possess one of the large arsenal of ballistic missile in the region , comprise primarily of SCUD - derive system .
Iran , North Korea and China have be willing provider of state - of - the - art technology .
compound this be the well - base suspicion that Syria have perhaps the most advanced chemical weapon capability in the Persian Gulf .
4 . China and the US economy
while the ominous possibility of heighten Iraqi chaos , missile in the gulf , and Syrian involvement loom large if the US attack Iran , all pale in comparison to the involvement of China in any US / Iran engagement .
_ economy be explode , hamper only by they great thirst for petroleum and natural gas to fuel they industry .
in the last several month , China have ink deal with Iran for $ 70 billion dollar worth of Iranian oil and natural gas .
China will purchase 250 million ton of liquefy natural gas from Iran over the next 30 year , will develop the massive Yadavaran oil field in Iran , and will receive 150000 barrel of oil per day from that field .
China be seek the construction of a pipeline from Iran to the Caspian Sea , where it would link with another plan pipeline run from Kazakhstan to China .
any US attack on Iran could be perceive by China as a direct threat to its economic health .
further , any fighting in the Persian Gulf would imperil the tanker run _ liquefy natural gas through the Strait of Hormuz .
should China decide to retaliate against the US to defend its oil and natural gas deal with Iran , the US would be face with a significant threat .
this threat exist not merely on a military level , though China could force a confrontation in the Pacific by way of Taiwan .
more significantly , China hold a large portion of the American economy in the palm of its hand .
Paul Craig Roberts , write for the American Conservative , say in July of 2005 that " as a result of many year of persistent trade surplus with the United State , the Japanese government hold dollar reserve of approximately $ 1 trillion .
_ accumulation of dollar be approximately $ 600 billion .
South Korea hold about $ 200 billion .
this sum give this country enormous leverage over the United State .
by dump some portion of they reserve , this country could put the dollar under intense pressure and send U.S. interest rate skyrocket .
Washington would really have to anger Japan and Korea to provoke such action , but in a showdown with China - over Taiwan , for example - China hold the card .
China and Japan , and the world at large , have more dollar reserve than they require .
they would have no problem teach a hegemonic superpower a lesson if the need arise . "
" the hard blow on American , " conclude Roberts , " will fall when China do revalue its currency .
when _ currency cease to be undervalue , American shopper in Wal - Mart , where 70 percent of the goods on the shelf be make in China , will think they be in Neiman Marcus .
price increase will cause a dramatic reduction in American real income .
if this coincide with rise interest rate and a setback in the housing market , American consumer will experience the hard time since the Great Depression . "
in short , China have the American economy by the throat .
should they decide to squeeze , we will all feel it .
_ strong hand in this even extend to the diplomatic realm ; China be a permanent member of the United Nation Security Council , and could veto any action against Iran propose by the United State .
5 . American preparedness
American citizen have for decade take it as a given that we military can overwhelm and overcome any foe on the battlefield .
the rapid victory during the first Gulf War cement this perception .
the last three year of the Iraq occupation , however , have sap this confidence .
badly , the occupation have do great damage to the strength of the American military , justify the decrease in confidence .
thanks to repeat deployment to Iraq and Afghanistan , recruiting be at a all - time low .
soldier with vital training and know - how be refuse to re-enlist .
across the board , the American military be stretch to the breaking point .
two vaunted economist - one a Nobel Prize winner and the other a nationally renowned budget expert - have analyze the data at hand and put a price tag on the Iraq occupation .
accord to Linda Bilmes of Harvard and Nobel Laureate Joseph E. Stiglitz of Columbia University , the final cost of the Iraq occupation will run between $ 1 trillion and $ 2 trillion , surpass by order of magnitude the estimate put forth by the Bush administration .
if a engagement with Iran envelop we force in Iraq , and come to involve Syria , we economy will likely shatter under the strain of fight so many country simultaneously .
add to this the economic threat pose by China , and the economic threat implicit in any substantial disruption of the distribution of Mideast petroleum to the globe .
if Iran and Syria - with they significant armament , missile technology and suspect chemical weapon capability - decide to engage with the relatively undersized US force in Iraq , we troops there will be fish in a barrel .
_ position over the gulf would make resupply by ship and air support from carrier a dangerous affair .
in the bad - case scenario , the newly - mint American order of battle require the use of nuclear weapon to rescue a surround and imperil force could come into play , hurl the entire planet into military and diplomatic bedlam .
conclusion : be any of this possible ?
the question must be put as directly as possible : what manner of maniac would undertake a path so fraught with peril and potential economic catastrophe ?
it be difficult to imagine a justification for any action that could envelop the United State in a military and economic conflict with Iraq , Iran , Syria and China simultaneously .
Iran be suspect by many nation of work towards the development of nuclear weapon , but even this justification have be toss into a cocked hat .
recently , Russian president Vladimir Putin bluntly state that Iran be not develop its nuclear capability for any reason beyond peaceful energy creation , and pledge to continue assist Iran in this endeavor .
therefore , any attack upon _ nuclear facility will bring Russia into the mess .
Iran also stand accuse of aid terrorism across the globe .
the danger implicit in any attack upon that nation , however , seem to significantly offset whatever gain could be make in the so - call " war on terror . "
unfortunately , all the danger in the world be no match for the self - assurance of a bubble - encase zealot .
what manner of maniac would undertake such a dangerous course ?
look no far than 1600 Pennsylvania Avenue .
George W. Bush and he administration have consistently undertake incredibly dangerous course of action in order to garner political power on the home front .
recall the multiple terror threat lob out by the administration whenever damaging political news appear in the media .
more significantly , recall Iraq .
Karl Rove , _ most senior advisor , notoriously tell Republican on the ballot during the 2002 midterm to " run on the war . "
the invasion of Iraq provide marvelous political cover for the GOP not only during that midterm , but during the 2004 presidential election .
what kind of political cover would be gain from a attack on Iran , and from the diversion of attention to that attack ?
the answer lie in one now - familiar name : Jack Abramoff .
the Abramoff scandal threaten to subsume all the hard - fight GOP gain in Congress , and the 2006 midterm be less than a year away .
be any of this a probability ?
logic say no , but logic seldom play any part in modern American politics .
all argument that the Bush administration would be insane to attack Iran and risk a global conflagration for the sake of political cover run into one unavoidable truth .
they do it once already in Iraq .
by Graydon Carter ( excerpt from " what _ lose " , publish by Little Brown )

what be a kimberwick bit use for ?
use as a help for horse that be quite strong puller while hack , hunt and do cross country .
it be a curb bit with a ported mouth piece and some horse appreciate this to give they more room in they mouth for they tongue .
it be not as precise as a pelham bit because it only use one rein , though the modern one have two or three slot on which to put the rein .
the low the rein , the strong the action and the low the rein the strong the action on the poll too .
useful for young kid who do not have big enough hand or the ability to handle two rein independently .
for horse that be strong puller .
it just give you a little leverage and curb pressure .
_ nice for horse that need a little more than a snaffle .
I know _ vague , but it depend on the horse .
the rider need to have independent hand as well , because you do not want to pull too hard on a bit like that . ;)

do the pop drying time slow down if it not expose to air ?
_ for a craft project ..... I want to use it the way u would use icing ....
take a bit of searching to discover that pop be probably pop - plaster of Paris and yes plaster of Paris will slow way down if it be not expose to air - in fact , if you be build up plaster ( " the way you would icing " ) to do sculpting , which be rather uncommon , you keep the set plaster damp in order to add more unset plaster or you have to wet the area where you will be add plaster " mud "
plaster of Paris do two thing
- it chemically set - get warm to hot then cool down and hard and
- it dry out , lose the water that be soak into the set structure
for example , a set plaster mold that be to be use for clay slip casting must be dry - it get wet pull the water out of the slip - while a set plaster mold use for molding wax must be soaking or damp wet http://www.mikegigi.com/castgobl.htm#lggobproj

I have a splitter / filter between my adsl and ph line ?
I have 2 phone run on the same line and the adsl which be connect to one of the phone and the filter , _ still get a buzzing noise even when I have disconnect the other phone without one .
why be it stil do this even though I _ have the other phone connect ?
would it be good if I get another filter and connect the other phone as well ?
turn the modem off and see if the sound be still there ... could be static on the line ... if the sound be still there with the modem off then the problem be not the dsl ....
if the trouble go away with the modem off , then make sure that everything except the modem be filter , this would include the alarm system , fax machine , satellite box , phone , etc ...
if everything be filter , and you still have this problem - try change the filter - if it be still there , try double up on the filter ...
you need either a filter for each device except the dsl modem , or a whole home filter which filter all the jack , except the one which the dsl modem connect .

hamster - will a hamster be ok live in the bathroom ?
in he cage in the bathroom ?
or would the steam from the shower be a problem ?
thanks d
if space be minimal , or you be keep he in there to be keep away from other pet , then I can understand why you would choose to keep he there .
there be some thing to consider though ...
rodent require special bedding in they cage to absorb they waste , and this need to be clean regularly , or you hamster could suffer from problem due the buildup of ammonia from he urine .
when you take a warm shower and build up steam , he cage will collect water , the bedding will absorb much of it , and will not be able to absorb the urine quite as it should .
you will also have to be wary of mold form on any toy or hide - away he may have .
you also _ want it get too warm for he too often .
overall , it be not a good solution , but you can keep he healthy and pull it off if you take the time to give he the extra care he will need because of it .
it may be a problem because the temperature be constantly change .
I would personally put he somewhere else .

how do I get to paris cdg airport to paris montparnasse ?
I have two option
use the metro or the air france bus
can anybody tell I if the metro run directly from CDG to montparnasse ?
if not what transfer should I get on ?
ty
on the RER / Metro :
in the airport , follow the sign that say " Paris by train " .
buy a ticket for Paris .
this will get you on the RER b line go into town .
stay on it until the " Saint - Michel Notre - Dame " station .
change there to the Metro 4 line go toward " Porte _ " .
get off at the " Montparnasse Bienvenue " station .
on the Air France bus :
as I recall , this bus drop you off near the Opera in Paris .
_ still have to take another bus or the Metro down to Montparnasse .
on the bus : get on bus 95 go toward " Porte de Vanves " .
buy a ticket from the driver .
stay on the bus until the " Montparnasse Bienvenue " stop .
on the Metro : get in the Metro at Opera .
take the 8 line toward " Balard " until the " Invalides " station .
change there to the 13 line toward " Chatillon Montrouge " and take it until the " Montparnasse Bienvenue " station .

how to start a new fish tank ?
_ get a 10 gallon for my betta tomorrow and I just want to know how to properly set it up .
_ still a beginner .

thanks .
when you get the tank make sure you wash the inside ( with plain water ) then you wash the gravel ( with only water too ) take out all the stuff that be float on top .
add only silk plant as plastic one may tear up you _ delicate fin .
you add the water and put water conditioner into the water .
start up you filter ( sponge filter be the good for betta ) and put in a heater and set it to anywhere between 78 - 82 .
wait about 2 week or 3 and test you water .
if everything be look good you may add you betta to its new home .
light be optinal since fish need the light turn off at night anyways and a air pump be not nessasary since they get air from the surface .
ask the people sell you the fish how you should set it up , they would know
add aquasafe with the water you put in it .
make sure the temperature be good .
do not put you fish tank close to the sun or alga grow in you tank .
everything else should be good .
make sure if you get new fish that they get along with one another .

question about the sinking of the Titanic ?
after the sinking of the Titanic in 1912 , be there a law make so that ship would carry enough lifeboat to save everybody on a ship if it be sink ?
if yes , be Canada involved in this act / law ?
sorry , _ just very nervous after watch the movie .
SOLAS ( Safety of Life at Sea ) , which be a international maritime treaty , come about in response to the tragedy of the Titanic .
today , it be the primary safety law affect virtually all ship , regardless of country of registration .
if you ever go on a cruise ship , you will be require to attend a SOLAS muster drill ( lifeboat drill ) within 24 hour of sailing .
most ship perform this drill before even leave the dock .
SOLAS cover just about every aspect of safety at sea , include minimum safety equipment , practice , and standard , lifeboat , navigation practice , fire protection , and so on .
we be much safe today on board ship due to SOLAS , and I suppose if any good come out of the Titanic tragedy , the adoption of SOLAS be probably it .
http://www.caribbean-cruising.net
--------------------------------------------------
edit : also I forget to mention early , most ( if not all ) cruise ship also practice lifeboat drill weekly , and it be not uncommon to see they to actually launch the lifeboat into the water as part of they drill when you be in port .
this not only ensure the lifeboat be operational and will work if need , but make the crew proficient at launch they .
I _ think so
_ worry .
when be the last time you hear about a ship sink ?

where in the world be Iguazu ?
Iguazu Falls
widely consider to be one of the most spectacular waterfall in the world , the Iguazu Falls on the border of Argentina and Brazil , be a certainly must see attraction in the area .
the centre of the falls be know locally as ' Garganta Del Diablo ' ( the _ Throat ) , where the huge volume of water send a constant mist of spray into the air .
with the sun shin down on the spray , create a rainbow in the foreground , this be the perfect place to get that trademark Iguazu Falls photograph .
however , save some of you shot for the rest of the fall , as in total there be around 270 cascade that spread out over nearly 2 mile of the Iguazu River .
the Iguazu Falls be easily accessible and , dependent on you time restriction and budget , you can get to the area by either bus or plane .
the near town to the site be Puerto Iguazu in Argentina , about 12 mile from the falls , and Foz do Igua√ßu in Brazil , which be equally close .
both town have airport that be serve regularly from the large city such as Sao Paulo , Rio de Janeiro and Buenos Aires .
the bus be obviously the cheap option , and travel up from Buenos Aires the trip be a full 20 hour , although the bus be very comfortable with spacious recline seat .
the bus trip down from Sao Paulo be a similar affair take around 18 hour .
Foz on the Brazilian side be the large town , however both be gear up to cater for visitor to the waterfall and national park , and so offer a range of accommodation for all budget .
for that with a large appetite for the scenery and a large budget , there be some hotel complex much close to the action with view of part of the fall .

what be Italian high Renaissance ?
have a look at this , it may help .
1 ) the Italian Renaissance begin the opening phase of the Renaissance , a period of great cultural change and achievement in Europe that span the period from the end of the 13th century to about 1600 , mark the transition between medieval and early modern Europe .
the term renaissance be in essence a modern one that come into currency in the 19th century , in the work of historian such as Jacob Burckhardt .
although the origin of a movement that be confine largely to the literate culture of intellectual endeavor and patronage can be trace to the early part of the 14th century , many aspect of Italian culture and society remain largely medieval ; the Renaissance do not come into full swing until the end of the century .
the word renaissance ( Rinascimento in Italian ) mean " rebirth " , and the era be well know for the renew interest in the culture of classical antiquity after the period that Renaissance humanist label the Dark Age .
this change , while significant , be concentrate in the elite , and for the vast majority of the population life be little change from the Middle Age .
2 ) the expression high Renaissance , in art history , be a periodizing convention use to denote the apogee of the visual art in the Italian Renaissance .
the high Renaissance period be traditionally take to begin in the 1490 , with _ fresco of the Last Supper in Milan and the death of Lorenzo de' Medici in Florence , and to have end in 1527 with the sacking of Rome by the troops of Charles V .
this term be first use in German ( hochrenaissance ) in the early nineteenth century , and have its origin in the " high style " of painting and sculpture describe by Johann Joachim Winckelmann .
[ 1 ] over the last twenty year , use of the term have be frequently criticize by academic art historian for over-simplify artistic development , ignore historical context , and focus only on a few iconic work .
[ 2 ]
hope it help !

what would you get if you cross a sussex male and a silkie female ?
I have a sussex male and a pekin female I buy 2 silky what would the sussex female and the silkie female would make ?
if you have any pic of you hen I would like to see they to compare they to mine thanks ?
a sussex cross with silkie would make a crossbreed * mutt * chicken .
there be a lot of genetics at play between a sussex and silkie , so the offspring would vary in appearance .
you _ say what color silkie or sussex you be deal with so I _ say what color you chick would be likely to be .
however , I can say what feature they would / could have .
feather type .
silky have hookless feather .
sussex have soft feather .
all offspring from this cross will have soft feather , as hookless feather be a recessive gene .
skin Color : silky have black skin color , which be dominate .
sussex have white skin which could be recessive or dominate .
either way rec. and dom. white gene dilute the black gene .
skin will be dark but light than the silky .
beard / muff : if you silkie have a beard / muff the offspring could have a beard as well , as this gene be incomplete dominate .
feathered foot / shank - chick could have feathered foot / shank as this be also incomplete dominate .
crest : chick could also develop a small crest due to this be another incomplete dominate gene .
comb type : silky have walnut comb which be actually genetically two comb type ( rose and pea ) single be also there , but be recessive .
so cross to a Sussex you could get a walnut , pea , rose , or single comb bird .
five toe : silky have five toe .
sussex have four toe .
cross together ( five toe be incompletely dominate ) chick could develop to have a fifth toe on both , or even one foot .
silkie cross be great bird , and very neat look .
hen make excellent mother as they be big , can see well , and be smart than silky .
good wish ,
Jamie / RhodeRunner

what be some unique custom in ireland ?
as far as _ aware we most unique custom would be the " country wake " .
in all my travels _ never see anything like it and be often meet with a odd look when I explain they to foreigner .
after a person die , they remains be " wake " in they home for roughly 2 - 3 day .
in this time visitor will come to the house , pay they respects to the desisted and they family and have a couple of cup of tea with a sandwich or a bun .
the wake also include the night sit where friend and family sit up through the night with the remains .
wake be common both north and south of the border with Protestant and Catholic alike .
but only really in the countryside .
the only notable difference I have notice be that in the south of Ireland one night of the wake be often hold in the chapel the night before the funeral , this tradition start after the civil war .
another unique custom ( and a die one at that ) be the Pioneer .
the Pioneer be a organization start at the end of the 19th century which push and support the ideal of temperance ( abstain from alcohol ) , in a attempt to deal with the massive issue of alcoholism that Ireland be grip by .
Pioneer take a pledge to remain tee - total and at the hight of the organization popularity , have a estimate two million member even fill Croke Park on the 25th anniversary .
I myself _ be one but appreciate that the organization be unlikely to make into the 22nd century .
the Orange Order and the 12th of July March would be argue by some not to be a Irish custom but unarguable tick every criteria to be consider one .
the march on the 12th of July be only really attend by Protestant in the Ulster but in spite of they be the large attend parade in Ireland .
barn brack and the ring .
the Irish custom we have in we family be ; we make sinnel cake for Easter , barn brack and col - cannon for Halloween .
Christmas cake for Christmas day .

be the San Francisco Bay Area mostly Caucasian back in the early 1970 ?
no .
there have be a large Asian presence in the SF Bay Area for a long time -- the Chinatown here be the large population of Chinese outside of China , there be lot of Japanese _ be displace during WWII .
the whole Western Addition and a large portion of the Haight be black .
the Mission be basically Latin - American .
as the Southeast Asian and Filipino come over , they add to the culture .
so , the Bay Area have be fairly mixed ethnically for a long time -- Caucasian may have seem to be a large populous but _ because most tourist back then be Caucasian and many of the hippie be Caucasian so _ who the photographer take picture of .
the other ethicity _ well represent in politics yet -- or rather , they be just break the color barrier in the 70' due largely to the more open - minded hippy generation .
Marin County be predominantly Caucasian and many of the expand outer east bay area start out as white suburb .
it be not so long after civil rights law against discrimination start to have a impact .
you never see black MUNI driver , Asian police , latino politician until then .
it be a evolution .
many illegal be not count in the population until the mid-80 .
we do not have big percent of Chinese migration until the mid 90 .
we have few people run across the Mexican border then .
we have few social benefit at that time for people so many immigrant be not count .
only Caucasian have any political power , corporate presence or own business except for mom and pop store in some neighborhood .
San Francisco be settle in the 19th and 20th century by mainly European immigrant except for some Asian worker who be manual laborer .
there have always be a Mexican - American cultural influence since Calif be own by Mexico .
we have a large black population in the 70 than we have now but they do not have any power until Willie Brown be elect .
San Francisco be always progressive and welcoming and tolerant to all kind of people historically .
the county outside San Francisco be more white than San Francisco in the 70 .
edit : my memory may not be good so you might get a more accurate answer from someone else who remember the time .

hi , I be a dog trainer for 25 year .
you need to purchase what be call a shoulder point harness .
this type of harness go around the _ chest and leg and have a clip for the leash up on the back of the dog in middle of shoulder blade .
this way , he _ reach the leash to chew it .
when he swivel he head to go for it anyway , tell he sharp " uh uh " gently correct he with a small tug and continue you walk .
do this repeatedly and frequently and he will learn to walk on a leash .
patience be the key here .
he be a young pup and will learn over time and consistency in he training .
and always , always train with love and positive method - never hit or harshly scold .
never train out of fear .
you want you dog to admire you as he pack leader , not fear you .
good luck with you puppy !
all the good .

how do you make you cat adjust to a new house ?
I and my family be move into a new house just outside a small town .
we be currently live a mile from the town in a house surround by field but the new house be beside a busy road .
we have have the cat for 10 year and _ want to leave it .
how could we make it settle in a new house .
you be not just move house - you cat be lose he territory .
territory be very important to cat , and they be very nervous when they go into a new place - a new house could be full of predator , or unknown menace - well at least he think so .
you will need to give he only a small place to explore , so he can make it he territory , and feel safe there .
then , he can have a place to retreat to when he feel scared .
you will need to get he box and bowl , and whatever blanket and toy be his , and smell like home , and put he in a room .
the room you sleep in be good ( see you so relaxed that you be sleep will send the message that everything be ok ) , but other will work just as well .
close the door , and keep he in there for a week .
he will feel much safe in that one room , than in a huge unknown house .
he will explore the room , mark everything with he cheek , and try to make it feel like he territory .
he will reassure himself that no other animal be in there , and that no other animal will come in - he be afraid that he be in someone _ territory when he be in a new house .
in a _ time , he will have make it his , and will be get more bored than afraid .
let he out for half a hour , to explore .
then put he back in .
he will be freak out , so go back to he territory will make he much happy .
extend the time he be out each day , but for the first month , always put he in he room at night , so he feel safe to sleep .
soon he will make the whole house his , but he need that one safe place to start from .
remember to visit with he while he be in the room , and tell he how good he be .
remember to give he the time he need to feel that the room be his - rush it , and he will be afraid of the whole house for a long time .
he might even start pee on thing in fear .
good luck with you new house and with he new territory !
let she explore when we move my cat have to explore the entire house before she feel comfortable .
in time though she / he will adjust . :)
they just do it on they own .

remember snake can go _ without eat .
in the winter , they will usually go deep underground and enter a hibernation - like state call brumation , which be characterize by a slowed metabolism and reduce activity .
king snake sometimes stop eat , particularly during the cool part of the year .
they have a natural instinct to hibernate .
if the snake be not pregnant or shed , and its enclosure be properly equip , a loss of appetite probably signal a beginning of hibernation .
hibernation be natural , and a necessity for snake that be go to be breed .
another thing that can cause a king snake to stop eat be shedding .
you can tell when you king snake be about to shed , because its eye will get milky look .
its body will be dull look , too .
in a few day the snake will begin to shed its skin .
for example , some snake will routinely go off they food in both the summer and winter , feed mainly in spring and fall .
_ natural and so long as you _ see any serious deterioration in they health be nothing to worry about .

bearded dragon question ... ?
I just buy a baby one yesterday .
I have a basking spot lamp that say it be a double reflector that focus 35 % more light / heat and provide beneficial uva ray important to the psycholical well - being of he .
my question be do that mean it give he not only the heat , but the " sun ray " he need ?
I also be wonder how long should this light be on .
the lady at pet smart say 4 hour , but on place on the net it say 10 to 12 hour .
_ get used to he new home , but _ eatin yet .
I have bearded dragon juvenile food and freeze - dry cricket .
any advice would be greatly appreciate .
thank you for you time .
let I try to break this down as simply as I can : diurnal ( active during the day time ) reptile like the bearded dragon require 3 type of " light , " uva , uvb , and heat .
any white light emit light source will emit uva , include heat bulb , _ the easy one to provide for .
uvb on the other hand can only be reproduce by a fluorescent source .
uvb will always be a separate bulb from the heat lamp , unless you use a mvb ( mercury vapor bulb ) which be the only reptile use bulb that will emit both uvb and heat from one bulb .
I highly recommend that you do not use coiled / compact uvb bulb as they be know to cause severe eye damage and / or blindness in reptile not to mention they have trouble maintain uvb output over time .
the long tube uvb bulb be good , like _ Repsitun model : http://lllreptile.com/store/catalog/reptile-supplies/uvb-fluorescent-lights-mercury-vapor-bulbs/-/zoo-med-24-repti-sun-100-fluorescent-bulb/ remember to replace uvb bulb accord to the _ recommendation after which time the bulb will no long produce uvb even if visible light still be .
so , to answer you question , no , if you just have a bulb that say it produce UVA then you do not have " the _ ray " that you bearded need .
you need to also provide a source of UVB lighting .
the person at Petsmart be very wrong ; in fact it be always a good idea to second guess what most pet store employee tell you ; they _ have the good track record regard give reliable pet care info .
UVB and bask temp ( should be about 110 F for a baby , 95 F for a adult ) should be available for 10 - 12 hour a day .
freeze dry food be not a good staple food source ; you need to offer live feeder insect .
bearded dragon be sight hunter , they need to see the food move to trigger a feed response , especially when they be baby .
Live food be also high in nutritional value than freeze dried .
cricket , silk worm , phoenix worm , and various feeder roach , like red - lobster , turkistan , and dubia , be good example of staple insect to offer you bearded .
Wax worm and meal worm should only be offer as treat item , for _ sake .
I would highly recommend that you read through some reliable beard guide to make sure you have everything set up correctly :
http://herp-info.webs.com/beardeddragon.htm
http://www.beardeddragon.org/articles/caresheet/?page=1
mm it depend on the size of he tank or cage or whatever you have he in .. at least as far as _ concerned .
if there be shady area he can move to ( for example a 3 x 5 x 4 tank with light on one side ) then you can leave it on a full 12 - 14 hour , if _ a small tank and he _ escape the light then 4 - 6 at most at a time though quite possibly 4 - 6 hour at a time twice a day .
either way you also need to keep a eye on the temperature if you be use a dry fish tank as ultra-violet light in my experience up the temperature significantly and without proper ventilation it can become a oven .
as to what the light provide it give ultra-violet ray .. which be important for health in lizard as it be in human .

when choose a parakeet look for a young one .
( the young the easy to tame ) look for clean smooth feather , beak , and clean vent feather ( the feather around the butt .. dirty vent feather mean the bird be not healthy ) look for a dark eye with no circle ( the old one have a circle ring in they eye ) .
look for a lot of stripe in they head that start from the beak and go back to the back of the bird .
the stripe be like hair the less stipe the old .
( think of a bald man lol ) look for clean feather .
if you want a boy the cere ( the nostril piece above the beak ) must be blue .
the girl have either pink or brown .
I would recommend that you get two parakeet .
but get either one male and one female , or two male .
do not get two female .
they sometimes _ get along ( you know how some girl be lol hahahaahh but for real though , two girl tend to fight a lot .
I have one yellow girl and a green and yellow boy .
they be the good !
if you choose to get a parakeet this be a trick that I use to tame they .
however if you plan on get one , then get more than one at the same time they need company .
my mom tell I how to tame they and I be very happy with the result .
it take I 4 day to get the new one to be able to step on and eat out of my hand .
this be the step I use .
honestly they have work for I twice with my parakeet .
hopefully they will work for you .
1 ) when you get the bird , place he or she or they in the cage .
leave they in there with food and water and such for about 2 hour .
2 ) then place you hand in the cage .
I take the cage and place it next to the couch .
then I sit on the couch , place one hand in the cage , hold a millet spray .
( this way they will associate you hand with food , and bird love food lol ) then I turn on the tv and watch .
this way they will see that you hand be good and _ not go to grab they or hurt they .
do this for about one hour .
( you can take break if you have to ) and repeat the step after about 2 hour .
3 ) after about day 2 , they will start to eat the millet spray from you hand .
( do not take away the food dish from the bird , they will associate you as the person who take away they food ) ....
then take you finger and place it under they belly , in front of they feet and say up .
push you finger to they foot gently and say up .
( the first couple of time they will fly all over the cage but as long as you _ jump back or screem they will get used to you ) they will have no choice but to go on you finger .
when they see that you _ harm they , they will go up on you finger when you say up .
4 ) if they be not go up by now you just _ keep try and keep try .
do not hit , yell , or harm they .
you have patience .
_ give up !
after a couple of week mine know when I say shoulder it mean to go on my sholder , when I say up it mean to jump up on my finger , when I say up and out it mean up on my finger and out of the cage .

people do not go to Ireland on holiday for the weather , it be unpredictable .
one thing you can be sure of about Irish weather be how little you can be sure of .
it may be shirtsleeve and sunglass in February , but winter woolly in March and even during the summer .
and then _ the rain .
Ireland receive a lot of rain , with certain area get a soaking as many as 270 day of the year .
County Kerry be the bad affect .
the southeast be the dry , enjoy a more continental climate .
the Irish weather work on the ' four season in a day ' principle , which basically mean that you _ predict a thing when it come to the behaviour of the sky .
some basic assumption , however , can be make .
in summer , from May to July , the day be reasonably warm and - most importantly - very long : at the height of summer you _ need to turn on light until after 10 pm .
it be also peak tourist season , which mean there be far more people just about everywhere but the most remote corner of the island , and price be at they high .
not surprisingly , most of the yearly festival occur during this time so as to take advantage of the crowd and the more favourable weather .
spring ( February to April ) and Autumn ( August to October ) make good alternative , although the _ ever - grow popularity as a tourist destination can often blur the line between mid - and high - season tourism .
still , you have a good chance of some peace and quiet , and the weather can be surprisingly good in April and September than in mid-July - again , _ all part of the uncertainty principle .
Spring festivity include the ever - popular St _ Festival .
although temperature do not often venture below freezing , winter ( December to February ) can be brutal , for huge part of the country - the west and northwest in particular .
crowd be at they thin , but many of the _ tourist attraction and service close down in October and _ reopen until Easter , which paradoxically leave visitor with a more convincing taste of how Ireland be experience by most of the Irish : _ cold , grey and dark by 5 pm , but _ always a pub to escape into when the rain start sheet down .
the thing to do be to bring the right clothing with you , clothes so you can layer up if it be cold and take off layer when it warm up .
waterproof clothing and footwear be essential plus a umbrella ..
as that famous Scotsman Billy Connolly say " there be no such thing as bad weather just the wrong clothes "
afraid I _ be more helpful , it be really a case of pot luck , although as the weather be so changeable often a cold wet morning will turn into a lovely warm sunny afternoon and evening or visa versa .

if you would like more on sex out Aplocheilus lineatus take a look at the discussion in the first source below .
if you have plant in you tank .
you lineatus be already spawn .

( _ even have a pair of killy leave egg on a float thermometer !

check out the second source .
I prefer dark color because I can see they egg , more easily and the fish look good next to they .
use a well rinse medicine vial , a cork , new fishing bobber or even a piece of non-crumbly styrofoam to float they .
there be a couple way one could spawn lineatus - mop spawn & water incubate they for two week , pick egg from a mop & put they in a tray of treated , seasoned water or set up the parent in a plant tank & move they so the fry can hatch out there .
if you have the room to separate the male ( s ) & female ( s ) , & feed they well on live food , ( assume that you be do weekly 50 % water change ) when you put they together they will leave a lot more egg .
just make up example , but if a pair be constantly together , they may lay 10 - 15 egg a day .
with extra blackworm and maybe freeze ( defrost , rinse ) freeze food early in the day , they may leave 30 - 40 egg at a time .
separate and feed extremely nourishing stuff , they may produce more .
separate a pair some time before a show ( killy be usually show & judge & often sell as pair ) will encourage they to court and show they good color .
they also start the day with no nick or ding in they fin .
the water change help with that too .
you also may need to treat the incubation water .
the chlorine and ammonia ( choramine ) be not good for the egg .
ironically sometimes it be wise to leave the newly pick egg in fresh tap water with some chlorination to kill microscopic critter that ride in with the egg .
then put the egg in water treat a couple of day before with a water treatment and leave open to " breathe " .
leave a jar with a dozen black worm in it will sate the _ desire for snack and they be more likely to leave fry or egg alone .
if a pair _ leave egg ... check the follow :
1 . be a tank mate ( such as another female killie or a cory or large snail ) rate the egg ?
2 . have we keep up with partial water change ?
3 . be there too much mineral in the water ?
aplo. lineatus be wide - spread over southern India .
that indicate that they thrive in different water chemistry .
still if you can get you pet shop to do a hardness or tds ( total dissolve solid ) test , that may give you a hint .
wing it a little here , a hardness of 100 to nearly 200 ppm ( part per million ) or 5.8 to 10.6 dh should be fine for gardnerus .
tds meter ( the thrifty _ hardness meter can be use if one have see one of you municipal water _ annual report .
they include a number of mineral there and you can figure out what percentage of that would be you hardness mineral ( calcium , magnesium and iron ) .
a number of mineral be not of much consequence .
however if there be a high level of sodium chloride ( common salt ) that can break down the chorion ( shell ) around the egg and allow critter to get in and eat the yoke and embryo . )
ironically sometimes it be wise to newly pick egg in fresh tap water with some chlorination to kill microscopic critter that ride in with the egg .
then put the egg in water treat a couple of day before with a water treatment and leave open to " breathe " .
if you get egg in the mail in a medicine vial , that be fine .
but get the egg out , maybe rinse in fresh tap water and then into the incubation water .
in time the egg can suffocate in the shipping container .
after a number of people begin complain about " mystery death " among incubate egg , some of the more advanced killie people begin suggest that after 7 - 8 day of incubation , one should do a 100 % water change - as the egg develop , they do release waste material .
another problem be that sometimes bad egg will fungus and the fungus will spread out and kill all the egg .
some people put in a very dilute Acriflaven solution to slow down the fungus , so one can take white egg out with a pipette or eyedropper .
other will add a drop of Methylene blue .
if a egg turn blue , it have die and then become dyed as the outer membrane break down .
get that out asap too .
